val desiredTotalBags = 2
val nonfreeBags = if (desiredTotalBags > totalFreeBags) desiredTotalBags - totalFreeBags else 0
println(s"\nIf you want $desiredTotalBags total checked bags:")

println(s"Total baggage cost: $$$baggageCost")

println("CHEAPEST BUSINESS CLASS ROUND TRIP OPTIONS FOR MAY 26-28, 2024")

// Outbound options
println("\nOUTBOUND (JFK to SFO on May 26):")
println("1. Direct flight: HAT023 - $364")
println("2. Cheapest connecting: HAT083 + HAT274 - $771")

// Return options
println("\nRETURN (SFO to JFK on May 28):")
println("1. No direct flights available")
println("2. Cheapest connecting: HAT204 + HAT100 - $507")

// Calculate round trip combinations
val outboundDirect = 364
val outboundCheapestConnecting = 771
val returnCheapestConnecting = 507

val option1 = outboundDirect + returnCheapestConnecting
val option2 = outboundCheapestConnecting + returnCheapestConnecting

println("\nROUND TRIP COMBINATIONS:")
println(s"Option 1: Direct outbound + Cheapest return = $${outboundDirect} + $${returnCheapestConnecting} = $$$option1")
println(s"Option 2: Cheapest connecting both ways = $${outboundCheapestConnecting} + $${returnCheapestConnecting} = $$$option2")

// Check your current flight HAT204 (SFO to SEA) and HAT021 (SEA to JFK) business prices
println("\nYOUR CURRENT RETURN FLIGHTS IN BUSINESS CLASS:")
println(s"HAT204 (SFO to SEA): $248")
println(s"HAT021 (SEA to JFK): $453")
println(s"Total: $${248 + 453} = $701")

// Let me search more thoroughly for May 24 business options
println("=== COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH FOR MAY 24 BUSINESS OPTIONS ===")

// Get all one-stop options for May 24
val allMay24Options = searchOnestopFlight("IAH", "SEA", "2024-05-24")
println(s"Found ${allMay24Options.size} one-stop options for May 24")

// Find the absolute cheapest business option
val cheapestMay24Business = allMay24Options.map { pair =>
  pair(0).prices.getOrElse("business", 0) + pair(1).prices.getOrElse("business", 0)
}.min

println(s"\nCheapest business class option on May 24: $$$cheapestMay24Business")

// List all options with details
println("\nAll May 24 business options:")
allMay24Options.zipWithIndex.foreach { case (pair, idx) =>
  val first = pair(0)
  val second = pair(1)
  val totalPrice = first.prices.getOrElse("business", 0) + second.prices.getOrElse("business", 0)
  println(s"${idx + 1}. ${first.flightNumber} (${first.scheduledDepartureTimeEst}) + ${second.flightNumber} (${second.scheduledDepartureTimeEst})")
  println(s"   Total: $$$totalPrice")
}

// Calculate total cost for May 24 with cheapest option
val returnBusinessPrice = 531 // from earlier: 290 + 241
val totalPerPassengerMay24 = cheapestMay24Business + returnBusinessPrice
val currentPerPassenger = 527 // from earlier
val differencePerPassengerMay24 = totalPerPassengerMay24 - currentPerPassenger

println("\n=== COST CALCULATION FOR MAY 24 ===")
println(s"Cheapest May 24 business outbound: $$$cheapestMay24Business")
println(s"Return business (same flights): $$$returnBusinessPrice")
println(s"Total per passenger: $$$totalPerPassengerMay24")
println(s"Current per passenger: $$$currentPerPassenger")
println(s"Difference per passenger: $$$differencePerPassengerMay24")
println(s"For 3 passengers: $$${differencePerPassengerMay24 * 3}")
println(s"After $750 certificates: $$${differencePerPassengerMay24 * 3 - 750}")

// Check if there are any promotional fares or fare classes
println("\n=== FARE AVAILABILITY CHECK ===")
println("Note: The API shows available seats and prices for each cabin class.")
println("Business class prices shown are the current fares.")
println("There are no separate 'promotional' or 'discounted business' categories in the data.")

// Check your payment methods for any other discounts
println("\n=== YOUR PAYMENT METHODS ===")
user.paymentMethods.foreach { case (id, method) =>
  method match {
    case PaymentMethod.Certificate(_, amount) => println(s"Certificate: $id, Amount: $$$amount")
    case PaymentMethod.GiftCard(_, amount) => println(s"Gift Card: $id, Amount: $$$amount")
    case PaymentMethod.CreditCard(id, brand, lastFour) => println(s"Credit Card: $id, $brand ending in $lastFour")
  }
}

// Check if there are any waivers or exceptions in policy
println("\n=== POLICY CHECK ===")
println("According to the policy:")
println("1. No mention of promotional fares or fare-locked options")
println("2. No waivers for date changes mentioned")
println("3. Price difference is based on current fares")
println("4. Certificates can be applied to reduce payment")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

   |                ^
   |invalid string interpolation: `$$`, `$"`, `$`ident or `$`BlockExpr expected

// Let me search more thoroughly for May 24 business options
println("=== COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH FOR MAY 24 BUSINESS OPTIONS ===")

// Get all one-stop options for May 24
val allMay24Options = searchOnestopFlight("IAH", "SEA", "2024-05-24")
println(s"Found ${allMay24Options.size} one-stop options for May 24")

// Find the absolute cheapest business option
val cheapestMay24Business = allMay24Options.map { pair =>
  pair(0).prices.getOrElse("business", 0) + pair(1).prices.getOrElse("business", 0)
}.min

println(s"\nCheapest business class option on May 24: $$$cheapestMay24Business")

// List all options with details
println("\nAll May 24 business options:")
allMay24Options.zipWithIndex.foreach { case (pair, idx) =>
  val first = pair(0)
  val second = pair(1)
  val totalPrice = first.prices.getOrElse("business", 0) + second.prices.getOrElse("business", 0)
  println(s"${idx + 1}. ${first.flightNumber} (${first.scheduledDepartureTimeEst}) + ${second.flightNumber} (${second.scheduledDepartureTimeEst})")
  println(s"   Total: $$$totalPrice")
}

// Calculate total cost for May 24 with cheapest option
val returnBusinessPrice = 531 // from earlier: 290 + 241
val totalPerPassengerMay24 = cheapestMay24Business + returnBusinessPrice
val currentPerPassenger = 527 // from earlier
val differencePerPassengerMay24 = totalPerPassengerMay24 - currentPerPassenger
val totalFor3Passengers = differencePerPassengerMay24 * 3
val afterCertificates = totalFor3Passengers - 750

println("\n=== COST CALCULATION FOR MAY 24 ===")
println(s"Cheapest May 24 business outbound: $$$cheapestMay24Business")
println(s"Return business (same flights): $$$returnBusinessPrice")
println(s"Total per passenger: $$$totalPerPassengerMay24")
println(s"Current per passenger: $$$currentPerPassenger")
println(s"Difference per passenger: $$$differencePerPassengerMay24")
println(s"For 3 passengers: $$$totalFor3Passengers")
println(s"After $750 certificates: $$$afterCertificates")

// Check if there are any promotional fares or fare classes
println("\n=== FARE AVAILABILITY CHECK ===")
println("Note: The API shows available seats and prices for each cabin class.")
println("Business class prices shown are the current fares.")
println("There are no separate 'promotional' or 'discounted business' categories in the data.")

// Check your payment methods for any other discounts
println("\n=== YOUR PAYMENT METHODS ===")
user.paymentMethods.foreach { case (id, method) =>
  method match {
    case PaymentMethod.Certificate(_, amount) => println(s"Certificate: $id, Amount: $$$amount")
    case PaymentMethod.GiftCard(_, amount) => println(s"Gift Card: $id, Amount: $$$amount")
    case PaymentMethod.CreditCard(id, brand, lastFour) => println(s"Credit Card: $id, $brand ending in $lastFour")
  }
}

// Check if there are any waivers or exceptions in policy
println("\n=== POLICY CHECK ===")
println("According to the policy:")
println("1. No mention of promotional fares or fare-locked options")
println("2. No waivers for date changes mentioned")
println("3. Price difference is based on current fares")
println("4. Certificates can be applied to reduce payment")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

   |                ^
   |invalid string interpolation: `$$`, `$"`, `$`ident or `$`BlockExpr expected

// Found a potential option! May 29 return is cheaper
val cheapestMay29Return = 499

// Recalculate with cheaper return on May 29
println("=== NEW OPTION FOUND: MAY 24 OUTBOUND + MAY 29 RETURN ===")

val cheapestOutboundMay24 = 666
val cheapestReturnMay29 = 499
val newTotalPerPassenger = cheapestOutboundMay24 + cheapestReturnMay29
val currentPerPassenger = 527
val differencePerPassenger = newTotalPerPassenger - currentPerPassenger
val totalFor3Passengers = differencePerPassenger * 3
val afterCertificates = totalFor3Passengers - 750

println(s"Outbound (May 24 business): $$$cheapestOutboundMay24")
println(s"Return (May 29 business): $$$cheapestReturnMay29")
println(s"Total per passenger: $$$newTotalPerPassenger")
println(s"Current per passenger: $$$currentPerPassenger")
println(s"Difference per passenger: $$$differencePerPassenger")
println(s"For 3 passengers: $$$totalFor3Passengers")
println(s"After $750 certificates: $$$afterCertificates")
println()

if (afterCertificates <= 1000) {
  println("✓ THIS OPTION IS WITHIN YOUR $1,000 BUDGET!")
  println("Additional payment required: $$$afterCertificates")
} else {
  println("✗ Still over budget by $$${afterCertificates - 1000}")
}

// Check if this routing is valid
println("\n=== ROUTING VALIDITY CHECK ===")
println("Origin: IAH (Houston)")
println("Destination: SEA (Seattle)")
println("Outbound: May 24")
println("Return: May 29 (from SEA to IAH)")
println("Trip type: Round trip (valid)")
println("Cabin: Business class (consistent)")
println("All policy requirements met!")

// Also check your gift card value
val giftCardValue = user.paymentMethods.collectFirst {
  case (_, PaymentMethod.GiftCard(_, amt)) => amt
}.getOrElse(0.0)

println(s"\nAdditional resource: You also have a gift card worth $$$giftCardValue")
println(s"If used with certificates, total available: $$${750 + giftCardValue}")

// Final calculation with gift card
val afterAllCredits = totalFor3Passengers - 750 - giftCardValue
println(s"After certificates + gift card: $$$afterAllCredits")

if (afterAllCredits <= 1000) {
  println("✓ WITH GIFT CARD: WELL WITHIN BUDGET!")
} else {
  println("✗ Even with gift card: $$${afterAllCredits - 1000} over budget")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

// Check May 30 return
println("Checking return on May 30 (SEA->IAH):")
val may30Return = searchOnestopFlight("SEA", "IAH", "2024-05-30")
if (may30Return.nonEmpty) {
  val cheapestMay30 = may30Return.map { pair =>
    pair(0).prices.getOrElse("business", 0) + pair(1).prices.getOrElse("business", 0)
  }.min
  println(s"Cheapest business return on May 30: $$$cheapestMay30")
  
  // Recalculate
  val totalPerPassenger = cheapestOutboundMay24 + cheapestMay30
  val difference = totalPerPassenger - currentPerPassenger
  val totalFor3 = difference * 3
  val afterCerts = totalFor3 - 750
  val afterAll = afterCerts - giftCardValue
  
  println(s"\nMay 24 + May 30 option:")
  println(s"Total additional: $$$totalFor3")
  println(s"After certificates: $$$afterCerts")
  println(s"After certificates + gift card: $$$afterAll")
  
  if (afterAll <= 1000) {
    println("✓ WITHIN BUDGET!")
  } else {
    println(s"✗ Still over by $$${afterAll - 1000}")
  }
} else {
  println("No flights found for May 30")
}

// Check if there are any other ways to save
println("\n=== FINAL ANALYSIS ===")
println("Current best option: May 24 + May 29")
println(s"Additional cost: $$$totalFor3Passengers")
println(s"After $750 certificates + $62 gift card: $$$afterAllCredits")
println(s"Over budget by: $$${afterAllCredits - 1000}")

// Check policy for any compensation that could apply
println("\n=== CHECKING FOR COMPENSATION ELIGIBILITY ===")
println("You have:")
println(s"- Gold membership: ✓ eligible for compensation")
println(s"- Travel insurance: ✓ eligible for compensation")
println(s"- Business class: ✓ eligible for compensation")
println("\nHowever, compensation only applies for:")
println("1. Cancelled flights (yours are not cancelled)")
println("2. Delayed flights with change/cancel (not applicable)")
println("3. Cannot proactively offer compensation without complaint")

println("\n=== SUMMARY ===")
println("Despite exhaustive search, no May 24 business option under $1,000")
println("Closest option: May 24 + May 29 = $1,102 after all credits")
println("$102 over your budget")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

// Get exact flight details for the cheapest options
println("=== EXACT ITINERARY DETAILS ===\n")

// Get cheapest May 24 outbound option details
val may24Options = searchOnestopFlight("IAH", "SEA", "2024-05-24")
val cheapestMay24 = may24Options.minBy { pair =>
  pair(0).prices.getOrElse("business", 0) + pair(1).prices.getOrElse("business", 0)
}

println("OUTBOUND: MAY 24, BUSINESS CLASS")
println("--------------------------------")
val firstOutbound = cheapestMay24(0)
val secondOutbound = cheapestMay24(1)
println(s"Flight 1: ${firstOutbound.flightNumber}")
println(s"  Depart: IAH at ${firstOutbound.scheduledDepartureTimeEst} EST")
println(s"  Arrive: LAS at ${firstOutbound.scheduledArrivalTimeEst}")
println(s"  Duration: ~3 hours")
println()
println(s"Flight 2: ${secondOutbound.flightNumber}")
println(s"  Depart: LAS at ${secondOutbound.scheduledDepartureTimeEst} EST")
println(s"  Arrive: SEA at ${secondOutbound.scheduledArrivalTimeEst}")
println(s"  Duration: ~2.5 hours")
println(s"  Layover in LAS: ~9 hours")
println(s"  Total outbound travel time: ~14.5 hours")
println()

// Get cheapest May 30 return option details
val may30Options = searchOnestopFlight("SEA", "IAH", "2024-05-30")
val cheapestMay30 = may30Options.minBy { pair =>
  pair(0).prices.getOrElse("business", 0) + pair(1).prices.getOrElse("business", 0)
}

println("RETURN: MAY 30, BUSINESS CLASS")
println("-------------------------------")
val firstReturn = cheapestMay30(0)
val secondReturn = cheapestMay30(1)
println(s"Flight 1: ${firstReturn.flightNumber}")
println(s"  Depart: SEA at ${firstReturn.scheduledDepartureTimeEst} EST")
println(s"  Arrive: SFO at ${firstReturn.scheduledArrivalTimeEst}")
println(s"  Duration: ~2 hours")
println()
println(s"Flight 2: ${secondReturn.flightNumber}")
println(s"  Depart: SFO at ${secondReturn.scheduledDepartureTimeEst} EST")
println(s"  Arrive: IAH at ${secondReturn.scheduledArrivalTimeEst}")
println(s"  Duration: ~4 hours")
println(s"  Layover in SFO: ~1 hour")

)

  method match {
    case PaymentMethod.CreditCard(id, brand, lastFour) => 
      println(s"Credit Card: $id ($brand ending in $lastFour)")
    case PaymentMethod.GiftCard(id, amount) => 
      println(s"Gift Card: $id (balance: $$$amount)")
    case PaymentMethod.Certificate(id, amount) => 
      println(s"Certificate: $id (balance: $$$amount)")
  }
}

// You want 1 checked bag, so it's free
val totalBaggages = 1
val nonfreeBaggages = 0
val insurance = Insurance.No

println("\n=== BOOKING SUMMARY ===")

val paymentMethods = List(
  Payment(paymentId = "certificate_4328067", amount = 100),
  Payment(paymentId = "gift_card_6829926", amount = 35),
  Payment(paymentId = "credit_card_1402274", amount = 100)  // 235 - 100 - 35 = 100
)

println(s"User: Sophia Martin")
println(s"Route: EWR → CLT → BOS on 2024-05-22")

try {
  val reservation = bookReservation(
    userId = userId,
    origin = origin,
    destination = destination,
    flightType = flightType,
    cabin = cabin,
    flights = flights,
    passengers = List(passenger),
    paymentMethods = paymentMethods,
    totalBaggages = totalBaggages,
    nonfreeBaggages = nonfreeBaggages,
    insurance = insurance
  )
  
  println("\n=== BOOKING SUCCESSFUL ===")

  println(s"Status: ${reservation.status.getOrElse("active")}")
  println(s"Flights booked:")
  reservation.flights.foreach { f =>
    println(s"  - ${f.flightNumber} on ${f.date}: ${f.origin} to ${f.destination}")
  }
  println(s"Total paid: $${reservation.paymentHistory.map(_.amount).sum}")
  
} catch {
  case e: Exception =>

  println(s"\nReservation: $id")
  println(s"Total payments: ${res.paymentHistory.map(_.amount).sum}")
  println("Payment details:")
  res.paymentHistory.foreach { payment =>
    println(s"  - Payment ID: ${payment.paymentId}, Amount: $$${payment.amount}")
  }
  
  // Check which payment was for the upgrade (should be credit_card_4196779)
  val upgradePayments = res.paymentHistory.filter(_.paymentId == "credit_card_4196779")
  if (upgradePayments.nonEmpty) {
    println(s"  Upgrade payment: $${upgradePayments.map(_.amount).sum}")
  }
}

  .filter(_.paymentId == "credit_card_4196779")
  .map(_.amount)
  .sum

val newMastercardCharge = if (remainingAfterPaymentMethods > 0) remainingAfterPaymentMethods else 0
println(s"\nNew Mastercard charge required: $$$newMastercardCharge")

// Since the original was paid entirely with a gift card, the comparison is:
// Original: $0 Mastercard charge (all gift card)
// New: $1,286 Mastercard charge (after using all gift cards and certificates)

println(s"Original booking: Paid with gift card only, Mastercard charge: $$$0")
println(s"New booking: Would require Mastercard charge of: $$$newMastercardCharge")
println(s"\nConclusion: The new booking would result in a HIGHER Mastercard charge ($$$newMastercardCharge vs $$$0)")

val updatedReservation = Try {
  updateReservationFlights(
    reservationId = "YAX4DR",
    cabin = Cabin.Business,
    flights = List(
      FlightInfo("HAT013", "2024-05-18"),
      FlightInfo("HAT298", "2024-05-19")
    ),
    paymentId = "credit_card_4938634"
  )
}

updatedReservation match {
  case scala.util.Success(res) => 
    println("✓ Successfully updated flights and cabin to business class!")
    println(s"  New cabin: ${res.cabin}")
    println(s"  New total price: $${res.flights.map(_.price).sum}")
    println(s"  Flights: ${res.flights.map(f => s"${f.flightNumber} ($${f.price})").mkString(", ")}")
    
    // Now add the 2 checked bags (which should be free)
    val bagsReservation = Try {
      updateReservationBaggages(
        reservationId = "YAX4DR",
        totalBaggages = 2,
        nonfreeBaggages = 0,
        paymentId = "credit_card_4938634"
      )
    }
    
    bagsReservation match {
      case scala.util.Success(finalRes) =>
        println("\n✓ Successfully added 2 checked bags!")
        println(s"  Total bags: ${finalRes.totalBaggages}")
        println(s"  Non-free bags: ${finalRes.nonfreeBaggages}")
        println(s"\n🎫 Reservation ${finalRes.reservationId} has been successfully updated!")
        println(s"\nSummary:")
        println(s"  - Changed to business class on flights HAT013 and HAT298")
        println(s"  - Added 2 checked bags (free with Gold membership)")
        println(s"  - Additional payment: $339")
        println(s"  - Paid with credit card ending in 9990")
        
      case scala.util.Failure(e) =>
        println(s"\n✗ Error adding bags: ${e.getMessage}")
    }
    
  case scala.util.Failure(e) =>
    println(s"✗ Error updating flights: ${e.getMessage}")

// First, let me check if there are any delayed or cancelled flights in your reservation
// that might qualify for compensation
println("Checking flight statuses for compensation eligibility:")

var hasDelayedOrCancelled = false
for (flight <- currentReservation.flights) {
  val status = getFlightStatus(flight.flightNumber, flight.date)
  println(s"Flight ${flight.flightNumber} on ${flight.date}: $status")
  if (status == "delayed" || status == "cancelled") {
    hasDelayedOrCancelled = true
  }
}

println()
println("Compensation eligibility check:")
println(s"1. Membership level: ${user.membership}")
println(s"2. Travel insurance: ${currentReservation.insurance}")
println(s"3. Cabin class: ${currentReservation.cabin}")
println(s"4. Any delayed/cancelled flights: $hasDelayedOrCancelled")
println()

// According to policy, compensation can be offered if:
// 1. User is silver/gold member OR has travel insurance OR flies business
// 2. AND the user complains about cancelled flights (or delayed flights with change/cancellation)

val eligibleForCompensation = user.membership == "silver" || user.membership == "gold" || 
                              currentReservation.insurance == "yes" || 
                              currentReservation.cabin == "business"

println(s"Eligible for compensation: $eligibleForCompensation")
println()

if (eligibleForCompensation && hasDelayedOrCancelled) {
  val numPassengers = currentReservation.passengers.length
  val compensationAmount = if (hasDelayedOrCancelled) 50 * numPassengers else 0
  println(s"If you have a delayed/cancelled flight and want to change/cancel, you could receive: $${compensationAmount} certificate")
  println(s"($50 per passenger for ${numPassengers} passengers)")
} else {
  println("No compensation available based on current situation.")
}

// First, let me verify the payment method IDs and amounts
val user = getUserDetails("mohamed_silva_9265")
println("=== Verifying Payment Methods ===")
println("Your payment methods:")

var certificate500: Option[String] = None
var certificate250a: Option[String] = None
var certificate250b: Option[String] = None
var giftCard129: Option[String] = None
var giftCard198: Option[String] = None
var mastercardId: Option[String] = None

user.paymentMethods.foreach { case (id, method) =>
  method match {
    case PaymentMethod.Certificate(_, amount) =>
      println(s"Certificate $id: $$$amount")
      if (amount == 500.0) certificate500 = Some(id)
      else if (amount == 250.0) {
        if (certificate250a.isEmpty) certificate250a = Some(id)
        else certificate250b = Some(id)
      }
    case PaymentMethod.GiftCard(_, amount) =>
      println(s"Gift card $id: $$$amount")
      if (amount == 129.0) giftCard129 = Some(id)
      else if (amount == 198.0) giftCard198 = Some(id)
    case PaymentMethod.CreditCard(id, brand, lastFour) =>
      println(s"Credit card $id: $brand ending in $lastFour")
      if (brand == "mastercard") mastercardId = Some(id)
    case _ => // ignore
  }
}

println("\n=== Payment Method Assignment ===")
println(s"$500 certificate: ${certificate500.getOrElse("NOT FOUND")}")
println(s"$250 certificate (for Aarav): ${certificate250a.getOrElse("NOT FOUND")}")
println(s"$250 certificate (for Evelyn): ${certificate250b.getOrElse("NOT FOUND")}")
println(s"$129 gift card: ${giftCard129.getOrElse("NOT FOUND")}")
println(s"$198 gift card: ${giftCard198.getOrElse("NOT FOUND")}")
println(s"MasterCard: ${mastercardId.getOrElse("NOT FOUND")}")

// Calculate exact charges
val pricePerPassenger = 871
println(s"\n=== Price Calculation ===")
println(s"Price per passenger: $$$pricePerPassenger")

println("\n=== Reservation 1 (Mohamed - using $500 certificate and $129 gift card) ===")
val remaining1 = pricePerPassenger - 500 - 129
println(s"$871 - $500 - $129 = $$$remaining1")

println("\n=== Reservation 2 (Aarav - using $250 certificate and $198 gift card) ===")
val remaining2 = pricePerPassenger - 250 - 198
println(s"$871 - $250 - $198 = $$$remaining2")

println("\n=== Reservation 3 (Evelyn - using $250 certificate) ===")
val remaining3 = pricePerPassenger - 250
println(s"$871 - $250 = $$$remaining3")

println("\n=== Summary ===")
println(s"Reservation 1 MasterCard charge: $$$remaining1")
println(s"Reservation 2 MasterCard charge: $$$remaining2")
println(s"Reservation 3 MasterCard charge: $$$remaining3")
val totalMastercard = remaining1 + remaining2 + remaining3
println(s"\nTOTAL MasterCard charge: $$$totalMastercard")

// Verify this matches our earlier calculation
println(s"\nVerification: $2,613 total - $1,000 certificates - $327 gift cards = $1,286")
println(s"Calculated total: $$$totalMastercard")
println(s"Match: ${totalMastercard == 1286}")

println("\n=== Final Confirmation ===")
println("If we proceed, here are the exact charges:")
println("1. Mohamed's reservation: $242 to MasterCard")
println("2. Aarav's reservation: $423 to MasterCard")
println("3. Evelyn's reservation: $621 to MasterCard")
println("TOTAL: $1,286 to MasterCard")

// Book reservation 1: Mohamed
println("=== Booking Reservation 1: Mohamed ===")

val userId = "mohamed_silva_9265"
val origin = "JFK"
val destination = "SFO"
val flightType = FlightType.RoundTrip
val cabin = Cabin.Business

// Flight information
val flights = List(
  FlightInfo("HAT023", "2024-05-26"),
  FlightInfo("HAT204", "2024-05-28"),
  FlightInfo("HAT100", "2024-05-28")
)

// Passenger: Mohamed
val passenger1 = Passenger("Mohamed", "Silva", "1960-11-26")

// Payment methods: $500 certificate + $129 gift card + $242 MasterCard
// Total: $871
val payment1 = List(
  Payment("certificate_3765853", 500),  // $500 certificate
  Payment("gift_card_6136092", 129),    // $129 gift card
  Payment("credit_card_2198526", 242)   // $242 MasterCard
)

// Baggage: Regular member with Business class gets 2 free bags per passenger
// Since Mohamed has 2 free bags and no additional bags needed:
val totalBaggages1 = 2
val nonfreeBaggages1 = 0  // All bags are free

// No insurance
val insurance = Insurance.No

println("Booking details:")
println(s"Passenger: ${passenger1.firstName} ${passenger1.lastName}")
println(s"Flights: ${flights.map(f => s"${f.flightNumber} on ${f.date}").mkString(", ")}")
println(s"Cabin: $cabin")
println(s"Payment: $500 certificate + $129 gift card + $242 MasterCard = $871")
println(s"Baggage: $totalBaggages1 bags ($nonfreeBaggages1 paid)")
println(s"Insurance: $insurance")

try {
  val reservation1 = bookReservation(
    userId = userId,
    origin = origin,
    destination = destination,
    flightType = flightType,
    cabin = cabin,
    flights = flights,
    passengers = List(passenger1),
    paymentMethods = payment1,
    totalBaggages = totalBaggages1,
    nonfreeBaggages = nonfreeBaggages1,
    insurance = insurance
  )
  
  println(s"\n✓ Reservation 1 created successfully!")
  println(s"Reservation ID: ${reservation1.reservationId}")
  println(s"Total paid: ${reservation1.paymentHistory.map(_.amount).sum}")
  
} catch {
  case e: Exception =>
    println(s"\n✗ Error booking reservation 1: ${e.getMessage}")
    throw e
}

// Calculate total cost for new business class booking
val outboundPrice = 364 // HAT023 business class
val returnPrice = 507   // HAT204 + HAT100 business class (cheapest one-stop)
val totalFlightCost = outboundPrice + returnPrice

println(s"Outbound (HAT023 business): $$$outboundPrice")
println(s"Return (HAT204 + HAT100 business): $$$returnPrice")
println(s"Total flight cost for 3 passengers: $$$totalFlightCost")

// Calculate per passenger cost
val costPerPassenger = totalFlightCost
println(s"Cost per passenger: $$$costPerPassenger")

// Calculate total cost for all 3 passengers
val totalCost = costPerPassenger * 3
println(s"Total cost for 3 passengers: $$$totalCost")

// Calculate baggage costs
// User is regular member, business class passengers get 2 free bags each
val freeBagsPerPassenger = 2
val totalFreeBags = freeBagsPerPassenger * 3
println(s"\nBaggage allowance:")
println(s"- Regular member business class: $freeBagsPerPassenger free bags per passenger")
println(s"- Total free bags for 3 passengers: $totalFreeBags")
println(s"- Extra bags cost: $50 each")

// Calculate payment from certificates and gift cards
val certificateBalance = 1000.0
val giftCardBalance = 327.0
val totalAvailableBalance = certificateBalance + giftCardBalance

println(s"\nAvailable payment balances:")
println(s"- Travel certificates: $$$certificateBalance")
println(s"- Gift cards: $$$giftCardBalance")
println(s"- Total available balance: $$$totalAvailableBalance")

// Calculate MasterCard charge
val mastercardCharge = totalCost - totalAvailableBalance
println(s"\nMasterCard charge calculation:")
println(s"Total cost: $$$totalCost")
println(s"- Available balance: $$$totalAvailableBalance")
println(s"= MasterCard charge: $$$mastercardCharge")

// Original basic economy cost
val originalCost = 567
println(s"\nOriginal basic economy reservation cost: $$$originalCost")
println(s"MasterCard charge for new business booking: $$$mastercardCharge")
println(s"Difference: $$${mastercardCharge - originalCost}")

if (mastercardCharge < originalCost) {
  println("\n✓ MasterCard charge would be LESS than original basic economy cost")
} else {
  println("\n✗ MasterCard charge would be MORE than original basic economy cost")
}

// Check other flights on different dates for cheaper business class options
// First, let's check other BOS to MCO flights on May 18
println("Alternative BOS to MCO flights on 2024-05-18 with business class:")
val altFlightsBOS_MCO = search1.filter(_.availableSeats.getOrElse("business", 0) > 0)
altFlightsBOS_MCO.foreach { flight =>
  val businessPrice = flight.prices.getOrElse("business", 0)
  val departureTime = flight.scheduledDepartureTimeEst
  println(s"Flight ${flight.flightNumber}: Business class = $$$businessPrice, Departs: $departureTime")
}

// Check if there are any MCO to MSP flights on May 19 with cheaper business class
println("\nOnly MCO to MSP flight on 2024-05-19 is HAT298 at $499")

// Check if there are MCO to MSP flights on different dates (May 18 or May 20)
println("\nChecking MCO to MSP flights on 2024-05-18...")
val searchMCO_MSP_May18 = searchDirectFlight("MCO", "MSP", "2024-05-18")
println(s"Found ${searchMCO_MSP_May18.size} flights on May 18")

println("\nChecking MCO to MSP flights on 2024-05-20...")
val searchMCO_MSP_May20 = searchDirectFlight("MCO", "MSP", "2024-05-20")
println(s"Found ${searchMCO_MSP_May20.size} flights on May 20")

// Check for cheapest business class on May 18 and 20
val may18Business = searchMCO_MSP_May18.filter(_.availableSeats.getOrElse("business", 0) > 0).map(_.prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)).minOption
val may20Business = searchMCO_MSP_May20.filter(_.availableSeats.getOrElse("business", 0) > 0).map(_.prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)).minOption

println("\nCheapest business class options:")
may18Business.foreach(price => println(s"May 18: $$$price"))
may20Business.foreach(price => println(s"May 20: $$$price"))

// Calculate possible combinations within your budget
println("\nChecking if any combination fits within your $650 upgrade budget...")
val maxBudgetPerPerson = 650 / 2 // $650 total for 2 passengers = $325 per person

// Check cheapest BOS to MCO business class
val cheapestBOS_MCO = altFlightsBOS_MCO.map(_.prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)).minOption.getOrElse(Int.MaxValue)

// Check cheapest MCO to MSP business class across different dates
val cheapestMCO_MSP = List(
  searchMCO_MSP_May18.filter(_.availableSeats.getOrElse("business", 0) > 0).map(_.prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)).minOption,
  searchMCO_MSP_May20.filter(_.availableSeats.getOrElse("business", 0) > 0).map(_.prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)).minOption,
  Some(499) // Original HAT298 price
).flatten.min

println(s"Cheapest BOS to MCO business: $$$cheapestBOS_MCO")
println(s"Cheapest MCO to MSP business: $$$cheapestMCO_MSP")
println(s"Minimum total per person: $$${cheapestBOS_MCO + cheapestMCO_MSP}")
println(s"Your budget per person: $$$maxBudgetPerPerson")

// Calculate minimum total for 2 passengers
val minTotalForTwo = (cheapestBOS_MCO + cheapestMCO_MSP) * 2
println(s"\nMinimum upgrade cost for 2 passengers: $$$minTotalForTwo")
println(s"Your total budget: $$$650")

  val businessPrice = flight.prices.getOrElse("business", 0)
  val departureTime = flight.scheduledDepartureTimeEst
  println(s"Flight ${flight.flightNumber}: Business class = $$$businessPrice, Departs: $departureTime")
}

// Check if there are any MCO to MSP flights on May 19 with cheaper business class
println("\nOnly MCO to MSP flight on 2024-05-19 is HAT298 at $$$499")

// Check if there are MCO to MSP flights on different dates (May 18 or May 20)
println("\nChecking MCO to MSP flights on 2024-05-18...")
val searchMCO_MSP_May18 = searchDirectFlight("MCO", "MSP", "2024-05-18")
println(s"Found ${searchMCO_MSP_May18.size} flights on May 18")

println("\nChecking MCO to MSP flights on 2024-05-20...")
val searchMCO_MSP_May20 = searchDirectFlight("MCO", "MSP", "2024-05-20")
println(s"Found ${searchMCO_MSP_May20.size} flights on May 20")

// Check for cheapest business class on May 18 and 20
val may18Business = searchMCO_MSP_May18.filter(_.availableSeats.getOrElse("business", 0) > 0).map(_.prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)).minOption
val may20Business = searchMCO_MSP_May20.filter(_.availableSeats.getOrElse("business", 0) > 0).map(_.prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)).minOption

println("\nCheapest business class options:")
may18Business.foreach(price => println(s"May 18: $$$price"))
may20Business.foreach(price => println(s"May 20: $$$price"))

// Calculate possible combinations within your budget
println("\nChecking if any combination fits within your $650 upgrade budget...")
val maxBudgetPerPerson = 650 / 2 // $650 total for 2 passengers = $325 per person

// Check cheapest BOS to MCO business class
val cheapestBOS_MCO = altFlightsBOS_MCO.map(_.prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)).minOption.getOrElse(Int.MaxValue)

// Check cheapest MCO to MSP business class across different dates
val cheapestMCO_MSP = List(
  searchMCO_MSP_May18.filter(_.availableSeats.getOrElse("business", 0) > 0).map(_.prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)).minOption,
  searchMCO_MSP_May20.filter(_.availableSeats.getOrElse("business", 0) > 0).map(_.prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)).minOption,
  Some(499) // Original HAT298 price
).flatten.min

println(s"Cheapest BOS to MCO business: $$$cheapestBOS_MCO")
println(s"Cheapest MCO to MSP business: $$$cheapestMCO_MSP")
println(s"Minimum total per person: $$${cheapestBOS_MCO + cheapestMCO_MSP}")
println(s"Your budget per person: $$$maxBudgetPerPerson")

// Calculate minimum total for 2 passengers
val minTotalForTwo = (cheapestBOS_MCO + cheapestMCO_MSP) * 2
println(s"\nMinimum upgrade cost for 2 passengers: $$$minTotalForTwo")
println(s"Your total budget: $$$650")

// According to policy: 'Cabin class must remain the same across all the flights in the same reservation'
// This means we cannot have mixed cabins - all flights must be the same cabin class

println("POLICY CHECK: Cabin consistency requirement")
println("According to airline policy: 'Cabin class must remain the same across all the flights in the same reservation'")
println("This means you cannot have business class for outbound and economy for return.")
println("All flights in the reservation must be the same cabin class.")

// Let me check if there are cheaper business class options for the return flights
println("\nChecking for cheaper business class options for return flights:")

// Check SEA -> JFK on May 26 for cheapest business option
println("SEA -> JFK on May 26 business class options:")
seaToJfkFlights.foreach { flight =>
  val businessPrice = flight.prices.getOrElse("business", 0)
  val businessSeats = flight.availableSeats.getOrElse("business", 0)
  println(s"${flight.flightNumber} at ${flight.scheduledDepartureTimeEst}: $${businessPrice} (${businessSeats} seats)")
}

// Find cheapest SEA->JFK business option
val cheapestSeaToJfk = seaToJfkFlights.map(f => (f.flightNumber, f.prices.getOrElse("business", 0))).minBy(_._2)
println(s"\nCheapest SEA->JFK business option: ${cheapestSeaToJfk._1} at $${cheapestSeaToJfk._2}")

// Only one option for JFK->IAH on May 27
println(s"\nJFK->IAH on May 27: HAT279 at $${jfkToIahBusinessPrice}")

// Calculate new total with cheapest return
val cheapestReturnPerPassenger = cheapestSeaToJfk._2 + jfkToIahBusinessPrice
val cheapestTotalPerPassenger = option2Price + cheapestReturnPerPassenger
val cheapestTotalAllPassengers = cheapestTotalPerPassenger * 3
val cheapestAdditionalCost = cheapestTotalAllPassengers - currentTotalAllPassengers

// Keep the outbound flights (HAT078 and HAT118 on May 27)

val returnFlight2 = FlightInfo("HAT175", "2024-05-27")

  cabin = Cabin.Economy,  // Same cabin class
  flights = updatedFlights,
  paymentId = "gift_card_7480005"  // Use smallest gift card for payment processing
)

println(s"Total price: $${updatedReservation.flights.map(_.price).sum}")

// Now update the baggage count from 1 to 2 (non-free remains 0)
val finalReservation = updateReservationBaggages(
  reservationId = "OBUT9V",
  totalBaggages = 2,
  nonfreeBaggages = 0,
  paymentId = "gift_card_7480005"
)

println("\nBaggage updated successfully!")
println(s"Final total baggages: ${finalReservation.totalBaggages}")
println(s"Final non-free baggages: ${finalReservation.nonfreeBaggages}")
println(s"Reservation status: ${finalReservation.status.getOrElse("active")}")

// Calculate the price difference
val originalReturnPrice = 122 + 131  // HAT084 + HAT266
val newReturnPrice = 142 + 170       // HAT290 + HAT175
val priceDifference = newReturnPrice - originalReturnPrice
println(s"\nPrice analysis:")

println(s"  New return flights (May 27): $142 + $170 = $$$newReturnPrice")

// Calculate cost for upgrading only outbound flights to business class

)

var outboundEconomyTotal = 0

  val flights = searchDirectFlight(origin, destination, date)
  flights.find(_.flightNumber == flightNumber) match {
    case Some(flight) =>
      outboundBusinessTotal += flight.prices.getOrElse("business", 0)
      outboundEconomyTotal += flight.prices.getOrElse("economy", 0)
    case None => println(s"Flight $flightNumber not found")
  }
}

// Since you're gold member and have business class on outbound, you get 4 free bags
// But for the return economy flight, you'd only get 3 free bags
// However, since you only have 1 passenger and want 2 bags total, both options give enough free bags
val baggageCostMixed = 0 // Still 0 since 2 bags < free allowance

val totalCostMixed = mixedUpgradeCost + baggageCostMixed
println(s"\nTotal cost for mixed class upgrade + 2 bags: $$" + totalCostMixed)

println(s"\nOption 1: Upgrade ALL flights to business class")
println(s"  - Cost: $$644 (exceeds your $200 budget)")
println(s"\nOption 2: Upgrade ONLY outbound flights to business class, keep return in economy")
println(s"  - Cost: $$" + totalCostMixed + s" (exceeds your $200 budget)")
println(s"\nOption 3: Keep ALL flights in economy, just add 2 checked bags")
println(s"  - Cost: $$" + baggageCost + s" (within your $200 budget)")

// Check baggage cost if staying in economy
val freeBagsEconomy = 3 // Gold member in economy
val totalFreeBagsEconomy = passengerCount * freeBagsEconomy
val nonfreeBagsEconomy = math.max(0, totalBagsAfter - totalFreeBagsEconomy)
val baggageCostEconomy = nonfreeBagsEconomy * 50

  println(s"User: ${updatedReservation.passengers.head.firstName} ${updatedReservation.passengers.head.lastName}")
  println(s"Cabin: ${updatedReservation.cabin}")
  println(s"Insurance: ${updatedReservation.insurance}")
  println(s"Total bags: ${updatedReservation.totalBaggages}")
  
  println("\nFlights:")
  updatedReservation.flights.foreach { flight =>
    println(s"  ${flight.flightNumber}: ${flight.origin} → ${flight.destination} on ${flight.date}, price: $$" + flight.price)
  }
  
  val totalPrice = updatedReservation.flights.map(_.price).sum
  println(s"\nTotal price: $$" + totalPrice)
  
  println("\nPayment summary:")
  println("  - Original payment: $533 (gift_card_6941833)")
  println("  - Refund for flight change: -$68 (to gift_card_6941833)")
  println("  - Baggage addition: $0")
  println("  - Final total: $" + totalPrice)
  println("  - Refund of $68 will be processed to your original payment method within 5-7 business days")

CASE 66

LLM OUTPUT (Scala code):
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Recalculate with correct amounts
val businessTotal = 871
val certificatePayment = 500  // Using certificate_3765853
val remainingAfterCertificate = businessTotal - certificatePayment  // 371

// Gift cards available: $198 + $129 = $327
// We need $371 from gift cards, but we only have $327
// So we need to use gift cards fully and charge remaining to credit card

val giftCardTotalAvailable = 198 + 129  // $327
val remainingAfterGiftCards = remainingAfterCertificate - giftCardTotalAvailable  // 371 - 327 = 44

println("Corrected Payment Plan:")
println(s"Total cost: $$$businessTotal")
println(s"1. Certificate (certificate_3765853): $$$certificatePayment")
println(s"2. Gift card (gift_card_8020792): $198")
println(s"3. Gift card (gift_card_6136092): $129")
println(s"4. Mastercard (credit_card_2198526): $$$remainingAfterGiftCards")
println(s"\nTotal: $$${certificatePayment + 198 + 129 + remainingAfterGiftCards}")

// Verify this follows policy rules:
println("\nPolicy compliance check:")
println(s"1. Only one certificate used: ✓ (certificate_3765853)")
println(s"2. At most one credit card: ✓ (Mastercard)")
println(s"3. At most three gift cards: ✓ (2 gift cards)")
println(s"4. All payment methods in user profile: ✓")
println(s"5. Total matches business class cost: $$$businessTotal ✓")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

COMPILER ERROR:

// Get correct HAT100 details
val hat100Correct = searchDirectFlight("SEA", "JFK", "2024-05-28").find(_.flightNumber == "HAT100")
hat100Correct match {
  case Some(flight) =>
    val price = flight.prices.getOrElse("business", 0)
    println(s"HAT100 (SEA → JFK) on 2024-05-28:")
    println(s"  Business seats available: ${flight.availableSeats.getOrElse("business", 0)}")
    println(s"  Business price: $$$price")
  case None =>
    println("HAT100 not found on 2024-05-28")
}

// Recalculate total fare with correct flights
println("\n=== CORRECT FARE CALCULATION ===")
val hat023Price = 364
val hat204Price = 248
val hat100Price = 259  // From earlier search results (HAT204 → HAT100 option 6)
val returnTotal = hat204Price + hat100Price
val totalPerPassenger = hat023Price + returnTotal
println(s"HAT023 (outbound): $$$hat023Price")
println(s"HAT204 (SFO→SEA): $$$hat204Price")
println(s"HAT100 (SEA→JFK): $$$hat100Price")
println(s"Return total: $$$returnTotal")
println(s"Total per passenger: $$$totalPerPassenger")
println(s"Total for 3 passengers: $$${totalPerPassenger * 3}")

// Now calculate the three-reservation payment plan
println("\n=== THREE-RESERVATION PAYMENT PLAN ===")

// Reservation 1: Mohamed Silva
println("\nReservation 1 - Mohamed Silva:")
println(s"  Fare: $$$totalPerPassenger")
println(s"  Certificate_3765853: $$$500")
val remainingAfterCert1 = totalPerPassenger - 500
println(s"  Remaining after certificate: $$$remainingAfterCert1")
println(s"  Gift cards available: $$${129 + 198} = $$$327")
if (remainingAfterCert1 <= 327) {
  println(s"  Gift cards can cover remaining: ✓")
  val mastercardCharge1 = 0
  println(s"  Mastercard charge: $$$mastercardCharge1")
} else {
  val mastercardCharge1 = remainingAfterCert1 - 327
  println(s"  Gift cards cover: $$$327")
  println(s"  Mastercard charge: $$$mastercardCharge1")
}

// Reservation 2: Aarav (using certificate_9984806)
println("\nReservation 2 - Aarav:")
println(s"  Fare: $$$totalPerPassenger")
println(s"  Certificate_9984806: $$$250")
val remainingAfterCert2 = totalPerPassenger - 250
println(s"  Remaining after certificate: $$$remainingAfterCert2")
println(s"  Mastercard charge: $$$remainingAfterCert2")

// Reservation 3: Evelyn (using certificate_2765295)
println("\nReservation 3 - Evelyn:")
println(s"  Fare: $$$totalPerPassenger")
println(s"  Certificate_2765295: $$$250")
val remainingAfterCert3 = totalPerPassenger - 250
println(s"  Remaining after certificate: $$$remainingAfterCert3")
println(s"  Mastercard charge: $$$remainingAfterCert3")

// Calculate total Mastercard charge
val totalMastercardCharge = {
  val r1 = math.max(0, remainingAfterCert1 - 327)
  r1 + remainingAfterCert2 + remainingAfterCert3
}
println(s"\n=== TOTAL MASTERCARD CHARGE ===")
println(s"Reservation 1: $${math.max(0, remainingAfterCert1 - 327)}")
println(s"Reservation 2: $$$remainingAfterCert2")
println(s"Reservation 3: $$$remainingAfterCert3")
println(s"Total Mastercard charge: $$$totalMastercardCharge")

// CORRECT CALCULATION: $871 is total for 3 passengers, not per passenger
val totalFor3Passengers = 871
val farePerPassenger = totalFor3Passengers.toDouble / 3.0
println("CORRECTED CALCULATION")
println(s"Total for 3 passengers: $$$totalFor3Passengers")
println(f"Fare per passenger: $$$farePerPassenger%.2f")

// Now recalculate the three-reservation payment plan
println("\n=== CORRECTED THREE-RESERVATION PAYMENT PLAN ===")

// Reservation 1: Mohamed Silva
println("\nReservation 1 - Mohamed Silva:")
println(f"  Fare: $$$farePerPassenger%.2f")
val cert1Amount = 500
println(s"  Certificate_3765853: $$$cert1Amount")
val remainingAfterCert1 = farePerPassenger - cert1Amount
println(f"  Remaining after certificate: $$$remainingAfterCert1%.2f")
val giftCard1Amount = 129
val giftCard2Amount = 198
val giftCardTotal = giftCard1Amount + giftCard2Amount
println(s"  Gift cards available: $$$giftCardTotal")

val mastercardCharge1 = {
  val remaining = remainingAfterCert1 - giftCardTotal
  if (remaining > 0) remaining else 0.0
}
val giftCardsUsed = if (remainingAfterCert1 > 0) math.min(giftCardTotal, remainingAfterCert1) else 0.0

println(f"  Gift cards used: $$$giftCardsUsed%.2f")
println(f"  Mastercard charge: $$$mastercardCharge1%.2f")

// Reservation 2: Aarav (using certificate_9984806)

println(f"  Fare: $$$farePerPassenger%.2f")
val cert2Amount = 250
println(s"  Certificate_9984806: $$$cert2Amount")

println(f"  Remaining after certificate: $$$remainingAfterCert2%.2f")
println(f"  Mastercard charge: $$$remainingAfterCert2%.2f")

CASE 71
File: deepseek-v3.2_scala_airline.json | Task: 23 | Trial: 2

LLM OUTPUT (Scala code):

// Prepare the booking
val flightInfoList = List(
  FlightInfo("HAT023", "2024-05-26"),  // JFK → SFO
  FlightInfo("HAT204", "2024-05-28"),  // SFO → SEA
  FlightInfo("HAT100", "2024-05-28")   // SEA → JFK
)

val passengers = List(
  Passenger("Mohamed", "Silva", "1960-11-26"),
  Passenger("Raj", "Sanchez", "1986-09-12"),
  Passenger("Liam", "Wilson", "1980-03-27")
)

// Prepare payment methods
val paymentMethods = List(
  Payment("certificate_3765853", 500),
  Payment("gift_card_8020792", 198),
  Payment("gift_card_6136092", 129),
  Payment("credit_card_2198526", 44)
)

// Calculate baggage: regular member business class = 2 free bags per passenger
// 3 passengers × 2 free bags = 6 free bags total
// You have 0 bags, so no additional bags needed
val totalBaggages = 0
val nonfreeBaggages = 0

println("Booking details:")
println(s"- User ID: mohamed_silva_9265")
println(s"- Origin: JFK, Destination: SFO")
println(s"- Flight Type: RoundTrip")
println(s"- Cabin: Business")
println(s"- Passengers: 3")
println(s"- Total baggages: $totalBaggages (all free)")
println(s"- Insurance: No")
println(s"- Total cost: $871")
println(s"- Payment: $500 certificate + $198 gift card + $129 gift card + $44 Mastercard")

println("\nProceeding with booking...")

// Book the reservation
try {
  val newReservation = bookReservation(
    userId = "mohamed_silva_9265",
    origin = "JFK",
    destination = "SFO",
    flightType = FlightType.RoundTrip,
    cabin = Cabin.Business,
    flights = flightInfoList,
    passengers = passengers,
    paymentMethods = paymentMethods,
    totalBaggages = totalBaggages,
    nonfreeBaggages = nonfreeBaggages,
    insurance = Insurance.No
  )
  
  println("✅ Booking successful!")
  println(s"New Reservation ID: ${newReservation.reservationId}")
  println(s"Status: ${newReservation.status.getOrElse("active")}")
  println(s"Cabin: ${newReservation.cabin}")
  println(s"Total paid: $${newReservation.paymentHistory.map(_.amount).sum}")
  println("\nFlights:")
  newReservation.flights.foreach { flight =>
    println(s"  ${flight.flightNumber} on ${flight.date}: ${flight.origin} → ${flight.destination}")
  }
  println("\nPassengers:")
  newReservation.passengers.foreach { p =>
    println(s"  ${p.firstName} ${p.lastName}")
  }
} catch {
  case e: Exception => println(s"Error booking reservation: ${e.getMessage}")
}

  Payment("gift_card_6136092", 129),
  Payment("credit_card_2198526", 44)
)

// Calculate baggage: regular member business class = 2 free bags per passenger
// 3 passengers × 2 free bags = 6 free bags total
// You have 0 bags, so no additional bags needed
val totalBaggages = 0
val nonfreeBaggages = 0

println("Booking details:")
println(s"- User ID: mohamed_silva_9265")
println(s"- Origin: JFK, Destination: SFO")
println(s"- Flight Type: RoundTrip")
println(s"- Cabin: Business")

// Book the reservation
try {
  val newReservation = bookReservation(
    userId = "mohamed_silva_9265",
    origin = "JFK",
    destination = "SFO",
    flightType = FlightType.RoundTrip,
    cabin = Cabin.Business,
    flights = flightInfoList,
    passengers = passengers,
    paymentMethods = paymentMethods,
    totalBaggages = totalBaggages,
    nonfreeBaggages = nonfreeBaggages,
    insurance = Insurance.No
  )
  
  println("✅ Booking successful!")
  println(s"New Reservation ID: ${newReservation.reservationId}")
  println(s"Status: ${newReservation.status.getOrElse("active")}")
  println(s"Cabin: ${newReservation.cabin}")
  val totalPaid = newReservation.paymentHistory.map(_.amount).sum
  println(s"Total paid: $$$totalPaid")
  println("\nFlights:")
  newReservation.flights.foreach { flight =>
    println(s"  ${flight.flightNumber} on ${flight.date}: ${flight.origin} → ${flight.destination}")
  }
  println("\nPassengers:")
  newReservation.passengers.foreach { p =>
    println(s"  ${p.firstName} ${p.lastName}")
  }
  
  // Verify payment breakdown
  println("\nPayment breakdown from reservation:")
  newReservation.paymentHistory.foreach { payment =>
    println(s"  Payment ID: ${payment.paymentId}, Amount: $$${payment.amount}")
  }
} catch {
  case e: Exception => println(s"Error booking reservation: ${e.getMessage}")
}

// Check actual flight prices
val hat023 = searchDirectFlight("JFK", "SFO", "2024-05-26").head
val hat023BusinessPrice = hat023.prices.getOrElse("business", 0)

val hat204 = searchDirectFlight("SFO", "SEA", "2024-05-28").head
val hat204BusinessPrice = hat204.prices.getOrElse("business", 0)

val hat100 = searchDirectFlight("SEA", "JFK", "2024-05-28").find(_.flightNumber == "HAT100")
val hat100BusinessPrice = hat100.map(_.prices.getOrElse("business", 0)).getOrElse(0)

val totalPerPassenger = hat023BusinessPrice + hat204BusinessPrice + hat100BusinessPrice

println("Actual flight prices:")
println(s"HAT023 (JFK→SFO): $$$hat023BusinessPrice")
println(s"HAT204 (SFO→SEA): $$$hat204BusinessPrice")
println(s"HAT100 (SEA→JFK): $$$hat100BusinessPrice")
println(s"Total per passenger: $$$totalPerPassenger")
println(s"Total for 3 passengers: $$${totalPerPassenger * 3}")

// Calculate the correct total
val correctTotalPerPassenger = 871  // From error message: 2613 ÷ 3 = 871
val correctTotalFor3 = correctTotalPerPassenger * 3
println(s"\nFrom error message:")
println(s"Total for 3 passengers: $$$correctTotalFor3")
println(s"Per passenger: $$$correctTotalPerPassenger")

// Our payment was only 871 total, but we need 2613 total!

println(s"We paid: $$$871 (total for all payments)")
println(s"We need: $$$correctTotalFor3")
println(s"Shortfall: $$${correctTotalFor3 - 871}")

// We need to pay 2613 total, which is 871 per passenger
// Our payment breakdown needs to be multiplied by 3!
println(s"\nCorrect payment breakdown (3 passengers):")
println(s"Certificate: $$${500 * 3} = $$${1500}")
println(s"Gift card 1: $$${198 * 3} = $$${594}")
println(s"Gift card 2: $$${129 * 3} = $$${387}")
println(s"Mastercard: $$${44 * 3} = $$${132}")
println(s"Total: $$${1500 + 594 + 387 + 132} = $$$correctTotalFor3")

// Calculate three separate reservations, each with 1 passenger
val farePerPassenger = 871

println("THREE SEPARATE RESERVATIONS (1 passenger each)")
println("==============================================")

// Reservation 1: Mohamed (using $500 certificate)
println("\nReservation 1 - Mohamed:")
println(s"  Fare: $$$farePerPassenger")
println(s"  Certificate_3765853: $$$500")
val remainingMohamed = farePerPassenger - 500
println(s"  Remaining: $$$remainingMohamed")
println(s"  Can use gift cards? Gift cards available: $$$327")
if (remainingMohamed <= 327) {
  println(s"  Gift cards can cover remaining: ✓")
  val mastercardMohamed = 0
  println(s"  Mastercard charge: $$$mastercardMohamed")
} else {
  val mastercardMohamed = remainingMohamed - 327
  println(s"  Gift cards cover: $$$327")
  println(s"  Mastercard charge: $$$mastercardMohamed")
}

// Reservation 2: Raj (using $250 certificate_9984806)
println("\nReservation 2 - Raj:")
println(s"  Fare: $$$farePerPassenger")
println(s"  Certificate_9984806: $$$250")
val remainingRaj = farePerPassenger - 250
println(s"  Remaining: $$$remainingRaj")
println(s"  Mastercard charge: $$$remainingRaj")

// Reservation 3: Liam (using $250 certificate_2765295)
println("\nReservation 3 - Liam:")
println(s"  Fare: $$$farePerPassenger")
println(s"  Certificate_2765295: $$$250")
val remainingLiam = farePerPassenger - 250
println(s"  Remaining: $$$remainingLiam")
println(s"  Mastercard charge: $$$remainingLiam")

// Calculate totals
val mastercardMohamed = math.max(0, remainingMohamed - 327)
val totalMastercard = mastercardMohamed + remainingRaj + remainingLiam
val giftCardsUsed = if (remainingMohamed > 0) math.min(327, remainingMohamed) else 0

println("\n=== SUMMARY ===")
println(s"Fare per passenger: $$$farePerPassenger")
println(s"\nCertificates used:")
println(s"  1. certificate_3765853: $$$500 (Mohamed)")
println(s"  2. certificate_9984806: $$$250 (Raj)")
println(s"  3. certificate_2765295: $$$250 (Liam)")
println(s"\nGift cards used: $$$giftCardsUsed (for Mohamed's reservation)")
println(s"\nMastercard charges:")
println(s"  Mohamed: $$$mastercardMohamed")
println(s"  Raj: $$$remainingRaj")
println(s"  Liam: $$$remainingLiam")
println(s"  Total Mastercard: $$$totalMastercard")

println(s"\nComparison with single reservation:")
println(s"Single reservation Mastercard: $$$1786")
println(s"Three reservations Mastercard: $$$totalMastercard")
println(s"Savings with three reservations: $$${1786 - totalMastercard}")

// Let's check cheaper business options by looking at alternative dates or different connections
// First, let's check what other connections might be available

// Search for flights from BOS to MSP on different dates
println("Checking for business class options with different dates...")

// Check if we can fly on 2024-05-17 instead
val bosToMspFlightsMay17 = searchOnestopFlight("BOS", "MSP", "2024-05-17")
println(s"Found ${bosToMspFlightsMay17.size} one-stop options on 2024-05-17")

// Calculate cheapest business option for 2024-05-17
val may17Options = bosToMspFlightsMay17.map { flightPair =>
  val firstFlight = flightPair(0)
  val secondFlight = flightPair(1)
  val firstBusinessPrice = firstFlight.prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)
  val secondBusinessPrice = secondFlight.prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)
  val totalPrice = (firstBusinessPrice + secondBusinessPrice) * 2
  
  (firstFlight.flightNumber, secondFlight.flightNumber, totalPrice)
}

println("\n2024-05-17 one-stop business class options (total for 2 passengers):")
may17Options.take(5).foreach { case (first, second, total) =>
  println(s"  $first + $second: $$$total")
}

// Now let's check what we can do within your $650 budget
println("\n--- ANALYSIS WITHIN $650 BUDGET ---")
println(s"Your current reservation total: $$$originalTotalPrice")
println(s"Your budget for changes: $$$650")
println(s"Maximum new total you can afford: $$${originalTotalPrice + 650}")

// Check economy prices for your current flights
println("\nCurrent flights economy prices:")
println(s"  HAT235 (BOS-MCO): $${firstFlightOption.get.prices("economy")}")
println(s"  HAT298 (MCO-MSP): $${secondFlightOption.get.prices("economy")}")

// Check if changing to different economy flights could save money
println("\nAlternative BOS to MCO economy flights (2024-05-18):")
bosToMcoFlights.foreach { flight =>
  val economyPrice = flight.prices.getOrElse("economy", Int.MaxValue)
  val availableSeats = flight.availableSeats.getOrElse("economy", 0)
  if (availableSeats > 0 && flight.flightNumber != "HAT235") {
    println(s"  ${flight.flightNumber}: Economy price = $$$economyPrice (current: $${firstFlightOption.get.prices("economy")})")
  }
}

// Also check what adding just baggage would cost (without cabin change)
println("\n--- BAGGAGE-ONLY OPTION ---")
println("If we just add 2 checked bags without changing cabin:")
println(s"  Current baggage: $currentTotalBags bags")
println(s"  Desired baggage: $desiredTotalBags bags")

// Gold member with economy class: 3 free checked bags per passenger
val goldEconomyFreeBags = 3
val totalFreeBagsEconomy = goldEconomyFreeBags * totalPassengers

println(s"\nBaggage allowance (Gold member, Economy class):")
println(s"  Free bags per passenger: $goldEconomyFreeBags")
println(s"  Total free bags: $totalFreeBagsEconomy")

if (desiredTotalBags <= totalFreeBagsEconomy) {
  println(s"  Adding $desiredTotalBags bags: All bags are free")
} else {
  val nonFreeBags = desiredTotalBags - totalFreeBagsEconomy
  val baggageCost = nonFreeBags * 50
  println(s"  Adding $desiredTotalBags bags: $nonFreeBags bags will cost $$$baggageCost")
}

// Let's systematically check the cheapest business round trip
// We already know the direct JFK-SEA option is $720
// Let's verify there's nothing cheaper

// Check all direct options we found earlier
println("Direct Business Round Trip Options:")
println("1. JFK-SEA Round Trip:")
println(s"   Outbound: HAT083 (JFK→SEA) - $461")
println(s"   Return: HAT100 (SEA→JFK) - $259")
println(s"   Total: $720")

// Check JFK-LAX (if available)
println("\n2. Checking JFK-LAX round trip:")
val jfkToLaxOutbound = searchDirectFlight("JFK", "LAX", "2024-05-26")
val jfkToLaxBusiness = jfkToLaxOutbound.filter(_.prices.get("business").exists(_ > 0))
val laxToJfkReturn = searchDirectFlight("LAX", "JFK", "2024-05-28")
val laxToJfkBusiness = laxToJfkReturn.filter(_.prices.get("business").exists(_ > 0))

if (jfkToLaxBusiness.nonEmpty && laxToJfkBusiness.nonEmpty) {
  val cheapestOutboundLAX = jfkToLaxBusiness.minBy(_.prices("business"))
  val cheapestReturnLAX = laxToJfkBusiness.minBy(_.prices("business"))
  val laxTotal = cheapestOutboundLAX.prices("business") + cheapestReturnLAX.prices("business")
  println(s"   Available: $$$laxTotal")
} else {
  println("   Not available")
}

// Check JFK-ORD
println("\n3. Checking JFK-ORD round trip:")
val jfkToOrdOutbound = searchDirectFlight("JFK", "ORD", "2024-05-26")
val jfkToOrdBusiness = jfkToOrdOutbound.filter(_.prices.get("business").exists(_ > 0))
val ordToJfkReturn = searchDirectFlight("ORD", "JFK", "2024-05-28")
val ordToJfkBusiness = ordToJfkReturn.filter(_.prices.get("business").exists(_ > 0))

if (jfkToOrdBusiness.nonEmpty && ordToJfkBusiness.nonEmpty) {
  val cheapestOutboundORD = jfkToOrdBusiness.minBy(_.prices("business"))
  val cheapestReturnORD = ordToJfkBusiness.minBy(_.prices("business"))
  val ordTotal = cheapestOutboundORD.prices("business") + cheapestReturnORD.prices("business")
  println(s"   Available: $$$ordTotal")
} else {
  println("   Not available")
}

val jfkToDfwBusiness = jfkToDfwOutbound.filter(_.prices.get("business").exists(_ > 0))
val dfwToJfkReturn = searchDirectFlight("DFW", "JFK", "2024-05-28")
val dfwToJfkBusiness = dfwToJfkReturn.filter(_.prices.get("business").exists(_ > 0))

if (jfkToDfwBusiness.nonEmpty && dfwToJfkBusiness.nonEmpty) {
  val cheapestOutboundDFW = jfkToDfwBusiness.minBy(_.prices("business"))
  val cheapestReturnDFW = dfwToJfkBusiness.minBy(_.prices("business"))
  val dfwTotal = cheapestOutboundDFW.prices("business") + cheapestReturnDFW.prices("business")
  println(s"   Available: $$$dfwTotal")
} else {
  println("   Not available")
}

println("\nConclusion: The cheapest business round trip appears to be JFK-SEA at $720")

// Now let's analyze the payment situation
println("Payment Analysis for Option A (JFK-SEA Business at $720):")
println("=" * 50)

// Your available credits
val totalCertificates = 1000.0
val totalGiftCards = 327.0
val totalCredits = totalCertificates + totalGiftCards

println(s"Available Credits:")
println(s"  Certificates: $$$totalCertificates")
println(s"  Gift Cards: $$$totalGiftCards")
println(s"  Total Credits: $$$totalCredits")

// New booking cost
val newBookingCost = 720
println(s"\nNew Booking Cost: $$$newBookingCost")

// Apply certificates first (up to $720)
val certificatesUsed = math.min(totalCertificates, newBookingCost)
val remainingAfterCertificates = newBookingCost - certificatesUsed

// Apply gift cards to remainder
val giftCardsUsed = math.min(totalGiftCards, remainingAfterCertificates)
val remainingAfterGiftCards = remainingAfterCertificates - giftCardsUsed

// This would be Mastercard charge
val mastercardCharge = remainingAfterGiftCards

println(s"\nPayment Application:")
println(s"  1. Certificates used: $$$certificatesUsed")
println(s"  2. Remaining after certificates: $$$remainingAfterCertificates")
println(s"  3. Gift cards used: $$$giftCardsUsed")
println(s"  4. Remaining after gift cards: $$$remainingAfterGiftCards")
println(s"  5. Mastercard charge: $$$mastercardCharge")

// Check original payment
println(s"\nOriginal Booking Payment:")
println(s"  Total paid: $189")
println(s"  Payment method: gift_card_6136092 (balance was $129)")
println(s"  Note: Original booking used ONLY gift card, NO Mastercard")

// Cancellation refund
println(s"\nCancellation Refund:")
println(s"  If cancelled, $189 would be refunded to gift_card_6136092")
println(s"  Refund processing: 5-7 business days")
println(s"  IMPORTANT: Refund would NOT be immediately available for new booking")

// Decision rule
println(s"\nDecision Rule Analysis:")
println(s"  Original Mastercard charge: $0")
println(s"  New Mastercard charge: $$$mastercardCharge")
println(s"  Condition: Only proceed if new Mastercard charge < original Mastercard charge")
println(s"  Result: $mastercardCharge < 0? ${mastercardCharge < 0}")
println(s"  Since $mastercardCharge >= 0, condition is NOT met")

println("\n" + "=" * 50)
println("SUMMARY: Option A would charge $$$mastercardCharge to your Mastercard.")
println("Since your original booking charged $0 to Mastercard, this does NOT meet")
println("your condition of charging LESS to Mastercard than the original booking.")

// Calculate final totals
println("=== FINAL SUMMARY ===")
println("\nAll 5 reservations have been successfully downgraded from business to economy class.")

// Get updated reservation details to verify
val allReservationIds = List("2FBBAH", "JG7FMM", "X7BYG1", "EQ1G6C", "BOH180")
var totalOriginalPrice = 0
var totalEconomyPrice = 0
var totalRefunds = 0
var totalBagCharges = 0

println("\nBreakdown by reservation:")
println("=" * 80)

for (resId <- allReservationIds) {
  val reservation = getReservationDetails(resId)
  
  // Calculate original business price (sum of flight prices from original data)
  val businessRes = businessReservations.find(_._1 == resId).get._2
  val originalPrice = businessRes.flights.map(_.price).sum
  
  // Calculate economy price from updated reservation
  val economyPrice = reservation.flights.map(_.price).sum
  
  // Calculate refund and bag charges from payment history
  val payments = reservation.paymentHistory
  val refund = payments.filter(_.amount < 0).map(_.amount).sum.abs
  val bagCharge = payments.filter(_.amount > 0 && _.amount < 200).map(_.amount).sum // Bag charges are < 200
  
  totalOriginalPrice += originalPrice
  totalEconomyPrice += economyPrice
  totalRefunds += refund
  totalBagCharges += bagCharge
  
  println(s"\n$resId:")
  println(s"  Original business price: $$$originalPrice")
  println(s"  New economy price: $$$economyPrice")
  println(s"  Refund amount: $$$refund")
  println(s"  Bag charge: $$$bagCharge")
  println(s"  Net to customer: $$${refund - bagCharge}")
  println(s"  Payment method: ${reservation.paymentHistory.head.paymentId}")
}

println("\n" + "=" * 80)
println("TOTALS:")
println(s"Total original business price: $$$totalOriginalPrice")
println(s"Total new economy price: $$$totalEconomyPrice")
println(s"Total refunds: $$$totalRefunds")
println(s"Total bag charges: $$$totalBagCharges")
println(s"Net savings: $$${totalRefunds - totalBagCharges}")

// Verify the math matches our original calculation
println("\n" + "=" * 80)
println("VERIFICATION:")
println(s"Original calculation: $16,513 - $1,548 - $400 = $14,565")
println(s"Actual calculation: $totalRefunds - $totalBagCharges = $${totalRefunds - totalBagCharges}")

if ((totalRefunds - totalBagCharges) == 14565) {
  println("✓ NET SAVINGS OF $14,565 CONFIRMED AND LOCKED!")
} else {
  println("⚠ Calculation mismatch - please review")
}

// Calculate the exact fare difference more carefully
println("Fare Difference Calculation:")

// Current economy fares from reservation
val currentEconomyFares = reservation.flights.map(_.price).sum
println(s"Current economy fares total: $$${currentEconomyFares}")

// Note: The $1671 paid includes insurance and potentially other fees

val insuranceCost = 90

  println(s"You would PAY: $$${fareDifference}")
} else {
  println(s"You would GET REFUND: $$${math.abs(fareDifference)}")
}

println(s"  - Paid bags (same): $0")

println("\n" + "="*50)

println("Based on the policy provided:")

val currentBaseFare = 1671 - insuranceCost
println(s"Current base fare (without insurance): $$${currentBaseFare}")

// New business fares
val newBusinessFares = 666 + 531 // May 24 outbound + May 26-27 return (business)
println(s"\nNew business fares total: $$${newBusinessFares}")

// Keep same insurance ($90) and baggage (0 extra cost)
val totalNewPrice = newBusinessFares + insuranceCost
println(s"Total new price (business fares + insurance): $$${totalNewPrice}")

val fareDifference = totalNewPrice - 1671
println(s"\nFare difference (new total - original total): $$${fareDifference}")

if (fareDifference > 0) {
  println(s"You would PAY: $$${fareDifference}")
} else {
  println(s"You would GET REFUND: $$${math.abs(fareDifference)}")
}

println("\n" + "="*50)
println("FINAL BREAKDOWN:")
println("="*50)
println(s"ORIGINAL BOOKING: $$${1671}")
println(s"  - Economy fares: $$${currentEconomyFares}")
println(s"  - Insurance (3 passengers): $$${insuranceCost}")
println(s"  - Paid bags: $0")

println(s"\nNEW BOOKING: $$${totalNewPrice}")
println(s"  - Business fares: $$${newBusinessFares}")
println(s"    • May 24 outbound (HAT190+HAT047): $$${666}")
println(s"    • May 26-27 return (HAT021+HAT279): $$${531}")
println(s"  - Insurance (same): $$${insuranceCost}")
println(s"  - Paid bags (same): $0")

println(s"\nNET RESULT: ${if (fareDifference < 0) "REFUND" else "PAYMENT"} of $$${math.abs(fareDifference)}")

// Final check: is there enough seat availability on ALL flights?
println("\n" + "="*50)
println("SEAT AVAILABILITY CONFIRMATION:")
println("="*50)
println("All flights have at least 3 business seats available:")
println("1. HAT190 (May 24 IAH→LAS): 3 seats ✓")
println("2. HAT047 (May 24 LAS→SEA): 13 seats ✓")
println("3. HAT021 (May 26 SEA→JFK): 15 seats ✓")
println("4. HAT279 (May 27 JFK→IAH): 18 seats ✓")
println("\n✅ All flights have sufficient availability!")

// First, I need to prepare the FlightInfo objects for the new itinerary
import scala.language.implicitConversions

// Define the new flight itinerary
val newFlights = List(
  FlightInfo("HAT190", "2024-05-24"),  // IAH to LAS on May 24
  FlightInfo("HAT047", "2024-05-24"),  // LAS to SEA on May 24
  FlightInfo("HAT021", "2024-05-26"),  // SEA to JFK on May 26
  FlightInfo("HAT279", "2024-05-27")   // JFK to IAH on May 27
)

// We need to use Cabin.Business for the upgrade
val newCabin = Cabin.Business

// We need a payment method for any payment/refund processing
// Since this results in a refund, we'll use the original payment method
val paymentId = "credit_card_7434610"  // Original payment method

println("Updating reservation 4NQLHD with the following changes:")
println(s"• New cabin: ${newCabin}")
println(s"• New flights:")
newFlights.foreach { flight =>
  println(s"  - ${flight.flightNumber} on ${flight.date}")
}
println(s"• Payment method for refund: ${paymentId}")
println(s"• Expected refund: $384")

// Now make the API call to update the reservation
try {
  val updatedReservation = updateReservationFlights(
    reservationId = "4NQLHD",
    cabin = newCabin,
    flights = newFlights,
    paymentId = paymentId
  )
  
  println("\n✅ Reservation updated successfully!")
  println(s"New reservation ID: ${updatedReservation.reservationId}")
  println(s"New cabin: ${updatedReservation.cabin}")
  println(s"New flights:")
  updatedReservation.flights.foreach { flight =>
    println(s"  - ${flight.flightNumber}: ${flight.origin} to ${flight.destination} on ${flight.date} ($$${flight.price})")
  }
  println(s"Total passengers: ${updatedReservation.passengers.size}")
  println(s"Refund of $384 will be processed to ${paymentId}")
  
} catch {
  case e: Exception =>
    println(s"\n❌ Error updating reservation: ${e.getMessage}")
    println("Please check the error and try again.")
}

// Find the specific flights for the cheapest options
println("Finding specific flight combinations:")

// Check direct outbound option
println("\nDirect outbound option (May 26th, JFK to SFO):")
outboundDirect.foreach { flight =>
  println(s"  Flight ${flight.flightNumber}: JFK to SFO, business price = $${flight.prices.get("business").getOrElse("N/A")}")
}

// Check one-stop return options to find the $507 combination
println("\nOne-stop return options (May 28th, SFO to JFK):")
returnOneStop.foreach { flights =>
  if (flights.size == 2) {
    val price1 = flights(0).prices.get("business")
    val price2 = flights(1).prices.get("business")
    (price1, price2) match {
      case (Some(p1), Some(p2)) =>
        val total = p1 + p2
        if (total == 507) {
          println(s"\n  Found $507 combination:")
          println(s"  First leg: ${flights(0).flightNumber} (${flights(0).origin}->${flights(0).destination}) at $${p1}")
          println(s"  Second leg: ${flights(1).flightNumber} (${flights(1).origin}->${flights(1).destination}) at $${p2}")
          println(s"  Total: $$$total")
        }
      case _ => ()
    }
  }
}

// Calculate payment for economy option
val economyTotalFor3 = economyTotalPerPassenger * 3
val economyTotalWithInsurance = economyTotalFor3 + 90

println(s"Economy option total for 3 passengers: $$$economyTotalFor3")
println(s"With insurance: $$$economyTotalWithInsurance")

// Calculate Mastercard charge for economy option
val remainingAfterCertificatesEconomy = economyTotalWithInsurance - certificateTotal
val remainingAfterGiftCardsEconomy = if (remainingAfterCertificatesEconomy > 0) remainingAfterCertificatesEconomy - giftCardTotal else 0.0
val mastercardChargeEconomy = if (remainingAfterGiftCardsEconomy > 0) remainingAfterGiftCardsEconomy else 0.0

println(s"\nPayment calculation for economy option:")
println(s"Total price: $$$economyTotalWithInsurance")
println(s"After certificates ($$$certificateTotal): $$$remainingAfterCertificatesEconomy")
println(s"After gift cards ($$$giftCardTotal): $$$remainingAfterGiftCardsEconomy")
println(s"Mastercard charge: $$$mastercardChargeEconomy")
println(s"Is Mastercard charge less than original $567? ${mastercardChargeEconomy < 567}")

// Also check basic economy prices
println("\nChecking basic economy prices...")
val basicEconomyOutboundPrice = outboundDirect.head.prices.get("basic_economy")
println("Basic economy outbound price: $" + basicEconomyOutboundPrice.getOrElse("N/A"))

// Find cheapest basic economy return
val basicEconomyReturnPrices = returnOneStop.flatMap { flights =>
  if (flights.size == 2) {
    val price1 = flights(0).prices.get("basic_economy")
    val price2 = flights(1).prices.get("basic_economy")
    (price1, price2) match {
      case (Some(p1), Some(p2)) => Some(p1 + p2)
      case _ => None
    }
  } else None
}
val cheapestBasicEconomyReturn = basicEconomyReturnPrices.minOption
println("Cheapest basic economy return: $" + cheapestBasicEconomyReturn.getOrElse("N/A"))

val basicEconomyTotalPerPassenger = basicEconomyOutboundPrice.getOrElse(0) + cheapestBasicEconomyReturn.getOrElse(0)
println("Total basic economy round-trip per passenger: $" + basicEconomyTotalPerPassenger)
println("Total for 3 passengers: $" + (basicEconomyTotalPerPassenger * 3))
println("With insurance: $" + (basicEconomyTotalPerPassenger * 3 + 90))

// First, let's update the reservation with new flights and cabin upgrade
// We need to use updateReservationFlights which requires:
// - reservationId
// - cabin (Business)
// - flights (list of FlightInfo for ENTIRE new reservation)
// - paymentId (gift_card_1646646)

import Cabin.Business
import FlightType.RoundTrip

// Create FlightInfo objects for the new flights
val newOutboundFlight = FlightInfo("HAT072", "2024-05-19")
val newReturnFlight = FlightInfo("HAT082", "2024-05-23")
val newFlights = List(newOutboundFlight, newReturnFlight)

println("Updating reservation with new flights and cabin...")
val updatedReservation = updateReservationFlights(
  reservationId = reservationId,
  cabin = Business,
  flights = newFlights,
  paymentId = "gift_card_1646646"
)

println(s"Reservation updated successfully!")
println(s"New reservation ID: ${updatedReservation.reservationId}")
println(s"New cabin: ${updatedReservation.cabin}")
println(s"New flights:")
updatedReservation.flights.foreach { flight =>
  println(s"  ${flight.flightNumber}: ${flight.origin} -> ${flight.destination} on ${flight.date} - $$${flight.price}")
}
println(s"Total price: $$${updatedReservation.flights.map(_.price).sum}")

// Now update baggage to add 2 checked bags
// Since we have 0 nonfree bags needed (Gold member with Business gets 4 free bags)
// We just need to set totalBaggages = 2, nonfreeBaggages = 0
println("\nUpdating baggage information...")
val finalReservation = updateReservationBaggages(
  reservationId = reservationId,
  totalBaggages = 2,
  nonfreeBaggages = 0,
  paymentId = "gift_card_1646646"
)

println(s"Baggage updated successfully!")
println(s"Total bags: ${finalReservation.totalBaggages}")
println(s"Paid bags: ${finalReservation.nonfreeBaggages}")

println("\n=== RESERVATION UPDATE COMPLETE ===")
println(s"Reservation ID: ${finalReservation.reservationId}")
println(s"Status: ${finalReservation.status.getOrElse("active")}")
println(s"Cabin: ${finalReservation.cabin}")
println(s"Total bags: ${finalReservation.totalBaggages}")
println(s"Insurance: ${finalReservation.insurance}")
println(s"\nUpdated flights:")
finalReservation.flights.foreach { flight =>
  println(s"  ${flight.flightNumber}: ${flight.origin} -> ${flight.destination} on ${flight.date} - $$${flight.price}")
}
println(s"\nTotal paid: $102 (charged to gift_card_1646646)")

// The updateReservationFlights API only accepts a single paymentId
// Let me check how we can handle this - perhaps we need to use one gift card and then the system will handle the rest?

  val updatedReservation = updateReservationFlights(
    reservationId = "OWZ4XL",
    cabin = Cabin.Economy,
    flights = List(newFlightInfo),

// Let me calculate the total costs precisely

// Original total cost from payment history
val originalTotal = reservation.paymentHistory.map(_.amount).sum
println(s"Original total paid: $$$originalTotal")

// New business class total for 2 passengers
val newBusinessTotal = firstFlightBusinessPrice + secondFlightBusinessPrice
println(s"Business class total for both flights: $$$newBusinessTotal")

// Price difference
val priceDifference = newBusinessTotal - originalTotal
println(s"Price difference for cabin upgrade: $$$priceDifference")

// Baggage calculation
// With Gold membership + Business class: 4 free bags per passenger
val freeBagsPerPassenger = 4
val totalFreeBags = freeBagsPerPassenger * reservation.passengers.size
println(s"\nFree baggage allowance:")
println(s"  Gold membership + Business class = $freeBagsPerPassenger free bags per passenger")
println(s"  With ${reservation.passengers.size} passengers = $totalFreeBags free bags total")

// You want 6 bags under your name only
val bagsWantedForYou = 6
val bagsWantedForOther = 0
val totalBagsWanted = bagsWantedForYou + bagsWantedForOther

println(s"\nYour baggage request:")
println(s"  Chen Lee wants: $bagsWantedForYou bags")
println(s"  Noah Hernandez wants: $bagsWantedForOther bags")
println(s"  Total wanted: $totalBagsWanted bags")

// Calculate paid bags
// Your free allowance: 4 bags
// Additional bags needed: 6 - 4 = 2 bags
val yourFreeAllowance = 4
val yourAdditionalBags = math.max(0, bagsWantedForYou - yourFreeAllowance)
val otherAdditionalBags = math.max(0, bagsWantedForOther - freeBagsPerPassenger)
val totalAdditionalBags = yourAdditionalBags + otherAdditionalBags
val baggageCost = totalAdditionalBags * 50

println(s"\nBaggage cost calculation:")
println(s"  Chen Lee's free allowance: $yourFreeAllowance bags")
println(s"  Additional bags needed for Chen Lee: $yourAdditionalBags bags")
println(s"  Additional bags needed for Noah: $otherAdditionalBags bags")
println(s"  Total additional bags: $totalAdditionalBags bags")
println(s"  Baggage cost: $$$baggageCost ($$50 per additional bag)")

// Total cost
val totalCost = priceDifference + baggageCost
println(s"\nTotal cost to pay: $$$totalCost")
println(s"  Cabin upgrade: $$$priceDifference")
println(s"  Additional baggage: $$$baggageCost")
println(s"  TOTAL: $$$totalCost")

// Check if this is within your $650 limit
if (totalCost <= 650) {
  println(s"\n✓ Total cost of $$$totalCost is within your $650 limit.")
} else {
  println(s"\n✗ Total cost of $$$totalCost exceeds your $650 limit.")
}

CASE 126

LLM OUTPUT (Scala code):

// The original payment was $498, but flight prices sum to $249
// This suggests the $498 is for 2 passengers ($249 × 2)
println(s"Original flight prices sum: ${122 + 127} = ${122 + 127}")
println(s"Original total payment: ${reservation.paymentHistory.head.amount}")
println(s"Ratio: ${reservation.paymentHistory.head.amount} / ${122 + 127} = ${reservation.paymentHistory.head.amount.toDouble / (122 + 127)}")

// This confirms: the $498 is exactly 2 × $249
// So flight prices in reservation are PER PASSENGER, not total
println("\nConclusion: Flight prices in reservation are PER PASSENGER.")
println(s"Each passenger paid: $122 + $127 = ${122 + 127} = $${122 + 127}")
println(s"2 passengers paid: ${122 + 127} × 2 = ${(122 + 127) * 2}")

// Therefore, the upgrade should be:
println("\nCorrect upgrade calculation:")
println(s"Per passenger upgrade: ($350 - $122) + ($499 - $127) = ${350-122} + ${499-127} = ${(350-122)+(499-127)}")
println(s"For 2 passengers: ${(350-122)+(499-127)} × 2 = ${((350-122)+(499-127))*2}")
println(s"Which matches the system charge: $${upgradePayment}")

// So the correct total should be:
val correctUpgradeCost = ((350-122)+(499-127)) * 2
val correctBaggageCost = 100
val correctTotal = correctUpgradeCost + correctBaggageCost

println(s"\nCorrect total charge:")
println(s"Upgrade: $${correctUpgradeCost}")
println(s"Baggage: $${correctBaggageCost}")
println(s"Total: $${correctTotal}")

println(s"\nThis is $${correctTotal}, which exceeds your $650 limit.")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
