// Find the cheapest combination for business class
val cheapestIahToLas = iahToLasFlights.map(f => (f.flightNumber, f.prices.getOrElse("business", 0))).minBy(_._2)
val cheapestLasToSea = lasToSeaFlights.map(f => (f.flightNumber, f.prices.getOrElse("business", 0))).minBy(_._2)
val cheapestSeaToJfk = seaToJfkFlights.map(f => (f.flightNumber, f.prices.getOrElse("business", 0))).minBy(_._2)
val cheapestJfkToIah = jfkToIahFlights.map(f => (f.flightNumber, f.prices.getOrElse("business", 0))).minBy(_._2)

println(s"Cheapest business class options:")
println(s"  IAH to LAS: ${cheapestIahToLas._1} - $$${cheapestIahToLas._2}")
println(s"  LAS to SEA: ${cheapestLasToSea._1} - $$${cheapestLasToSea._2}")
println(s"  SEA to JFK: ${cheapestSeaToJfk._1} - $$${cheapestSeaToJfk._2}")
println(s"  JFK to IAH: ${cheapestJfkToIah._1} - $$${cheapestJfkToIah._2}")

val cheapestTotal = cheapestIahToLas._2 + cheapestLasToSea._2 + cheapestSeaToJfk._2 + cheapestJfkToIah._2
val cheapestTotal3Passengers = cheapestTotal * 3
val cheapestDifference = cheapestTotal3Passengers - currentTotal3Passengers

println(s"\nCheapest business class total (base fare): $$$cheapestTotal × 3 = $$$cheapestTotal3Passengers")
println(s"Price difference from current: $$$cheapestDifference")

// Check if we can get under $1,000 difference
if (cheapestDifference <= 1000) {
  println(s"\n✓ This combination would keep the extra cost under $1,000!")
} else {
  println(s"\n✗ Even the cheapest business class combination exceeds $1,000 extra cost.")
}

println(s"  LAS to SEA: ${cheapestLasToSea._1} - $$${cheapestLasToSea._2}")
println(s"  SEA to JFK: ${cheapestSeaToJfk._1} - $$${cheapestSeaToJfk._2}")
println(s"  JFK to IAH: ${cheapestJfkToIah._1} - $$${cheapestJfkToIah._2}")

val cheapestTotal = cheapestIahToLas._2 + cheapestLasToSea._2 + cheapestSeaToJfk._2 + cheapestJfkToIah._2
val cheapestTotal3Passengers = cheapestTotal * 3
val cheapestDifference = cheapestTotal3Passengers - currentTotal3Passengers

println(s"\nCheapest business class total (base fare): $$$cheapestTotal × 3 = $$$cheapestTotal3Passengers")
println(s"Price difference from current: $$$cheapestDifference")

// Check if we can get under $1,000 difference
if (cheapestDifference <= 1000) {
  println(s"\n✓ This combination would keep the extra cost under $$$1,000!")
} else {
  println(s"\n✗ Even the cheapest business class combination exceeds $$$1,000 extra cost.")
}

// Let's explore more date combinations to find the absolute cheapest
println("Exploring different date combinations for business class...")

// Check IAH to SEA on May 23 (current date) - maybe cheaper business class?
val iahToSeaMay23 = searchDirectFlight("IAH", "SEA", "2024-05-23")
val cheapestIahToSeaMay23 = if (iahToSeaMay23.nonEmpty) {
  iahToSeaMay23.map(f => f.prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)).min
} else {
  // Check one-stop
  val oneStopMay23 = searchOnestopFlight("IAH", "SEA", "2024-05-23")
  if (oneStopMay23.nonEmpty) {
    oneStopMay23.map { pair =>
      pair(0).prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue) + pair(1).prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)
    }.min
  } else Int.MaxValue
}
println(s"Cheapest IAH→SEA business class on May 23: $${cheapestIahToSeaMay23}")

// Check IAH to SEA on May 25
val iahToSeaMay25 = searchDirectFlight("IAH", "SEA", "2024-05-25")
val cheapestIahToSeaMay25 = if (iahToSeaMay25.nonEmpty) {
  iahToSeaMay25.map(f => f.prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)).min
} else {
  val oneStopMay25 = searchOnestopFlight("IAH", "SEA", "2024-05-25")
  if (oneStopMay25.nonEmpty) {
    oneStopMay25.map { pair =>
      pair(0).prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue) + pair(1).prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)
    }.min
  } else Int.MaxValue
}
println(s"Cheapest IAH→SEA business class on May 25: $${cheapestIahToSeaMay25}")

// Check SEA to JFK on May 27
val seaToJfkMay27 = searchDirectFlight("SEA", "JFK", "2024-05-27")
val cheapestSeaToJfkMay27 = if (seaToJfkMay27.nonEmpty) {
  seaToJfkMay27.map(f => f.prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)).min
} else Int.MaxValue
println(s"Cheapest SEA→JFK business class on May 27: $${cheapestSeaToJfkMay27}")

// Check JFK to IAH on May 26
val jfkToIahMay26 = searchDirectFlight("JFK", "IAH", "2024-05-26")
val cheapestJfkToIahMay26 = if (jfkToIahMay26.nonEmpty) {
  jfkToIahMay26.map(f => f.prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)).min
} else Int.MaxValue
println(s"Cheapest JFK→IAH business class on May 26: $${cheapestJfkToIahMay26}")

// Find the absolute cheapest combination
val dateCombinations = List(
  ("May 23-26-27", cheapestIahToSeaMay23 + cheapestSeaToJfkMay27 + cheapestJfkToIahMay28Price),
  ("May 24-25-28", cheapestOneStopPrice + cheapestSeaToJfkMay25Price + cheapestJfkToIahMay28Price),
  ("May 24-26-27", cheapestOneStopPrice + cheapestSeaToJfkMay25Price + cheapestJfkToIahMay28Price), // Using May 26 SEA->JFK
  ("May 25-26-28", cheapestIahToSeaMay25 + cheapestSeaToJfkMay27 + cheapestJfkToIahMay28Price)
)

println("\nCheapest combinations found:")
dateCombinations.foreach { case (dates, total) =>
  if (total < Int.MaxValue) {
    val total3Passengers = total * 3
    val difference = total3Passengers - currentTotal3Passengers
    val outOfPocket = difference - (totalCertificateValue + totalGiftCardValue)
    println(s"  $dates: $${total} per passenger, out-of-pocket: $$$outOfPocket")
  }
}

// Check if any combination gets under $1,000 out-of-pocket
val bestCombination = dateCombinations.filter(_._2 < Int.MaxValue).minBy { case (_, total) =>
  val total3Passengers = total * 3
  val difference = total3Passengers - currentTotal3Passengers
  difference - (totalCertificateValue + totalGiftCardValue)
}

val bestTotal = bestCombination._2
val bestTotal3Passengers = bestTotal * 3
val bestDifference = bestTotal3Passengers - currentTotal3Passengers
val bestOutOfPocket = bestDifference - (totalCertificateValue + totalGiftCardValue)

println(s"\nBest combination: ${bestCombination._1}")
println(s"Out-of-pocket cost: $$$bestOutOfPocket")

if (bestOutOfPocket <= 1000) {
  println("\n✓ Found a combination within your $1,000 budget!")
} else {
  println(s"\n✗ Even the cheapest combination exceeds your $1,000 budget by $$${bestOutOfPocket - 1000}")
}

// Get actual numbers for the cheapest combinations

println(s"  4. May 25-27-28: $${combo4}")

// Calculate out-of-pocket for each
def calculateOutOfPocket(totalPerPassenger: Int): Double = {
  val total3Passengers = totalPerPassenger * 3
  val difference = total3Passengers - currentTotal3Passengers
  difference - (totalCertificateValue + totalGiftCardValue)
}

println(s"\nOut-of-pocket costs:")
println(s"  1. May 23-27-28: $${calculateOutOfPocket(combo1)}")
println(s"  2. May 24-25-28: $${calculateOutOfPocket(combo2)}")
println(s"  3. May 24-26-28: $${calculateOutOfPocket(combo3)}")
println(s"  4. May 25-27-28: $${calculateOutOfPocket(combo4)}")

// Find the absolute minimum
val allCombinations = List(combo1, combo2, combo3, combo4).filter(_ < Int.MaxValue)
val minCombination = allCombinations.min
val minOutOfPocket = calculateOutOfPocket(minCombination)

println(s"\nMinimum out-of-pocket cost: $${minOutOfPocket}")

// Let me recalculate everything in one go
println("Searching for the absolute cheapest business class combination...")

// Search for all needed flights
val iahToSeaMay23Direct = searchDirectFlight("IAH", "SEA", "2024-05-23")
val iahToSeaMay23OneStop = searchOnestopFlight("IAH", "SEA", "2024-05-23")
val cheapestIahToSeaMay23 = {
  val directPrice = if (iahToSeaMay23Direct.nonEmpty) iahToSeaMay23Direct.map(_.prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)).min else Int.MaxValue
  val oneStopPrice = if (iahToSeaMay23OneStop.nonEmpty) iahToSeaMay23OneStop.map(pair => pair(0).prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue) + pair(1).prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)).min else Int.MaxValue
  math.min(directPrice, oneStopPrice)
}

val iahToSeaMay25Direct = searchDirectFlight("IAH", "SEA", "2024-05-25")
val iahToSeaMay25OneStop = searchOnestopFlight("IAH", "SEA", "2024-05-25")

  val oneStopPrice = if (iahToSeaMay25OneStop.nonEmpty) iahToSeaMay25OneStop.map(pair => pair(0).prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue) + pair(1).prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)).min else Int.MaxValue
  math.min(directPrice, oneStopPrice)
}

val seaToJfkMay27 = searchDirectFlight("SEA", "JFK", "2024-05-27")

// Do a comprehensive search for the cheapest business class combination
println("Comprehensive search for cheapest business class options...")

// Define current total
val currentTotalPerPassenger = 527  // $1581 / 3
val currentTotal3Passengers = currentTotalPerPassenger * 3

// Define discount amounts
val totalDiscounts = 750.0 + 62.0  // $812 total

// Search for all flight options
// IAH to SEA options
val iahToSeaMay23Price = {
  val direct = searchDirectFlight("IAH", "SEA", "2024-05-23")
  val oneStop = searchOnestopFlight("IAH", "SEA", "2024-05-23")
  val directMin = if (direct.nonEmpty) direct.map(_.prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)).min else Int.MaxValue
  val oneStopMin = if (oneStop.nonEmpty) oneStop.map(p => p(0).prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue) + p(1).prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)).min else Int.MaxValue
  math.min(directMin, oneStopMin)
}

val iahToSeaMay24Price = cheapestOneStopPrice  // $666 from earlier search
val iahToSeaMay25Price = {
  val direct = searchDirectFlight("IAH", "SEA", "2024-05-25")
  val oneStop = searchOnestopFlight("IAH", "SEA", "2024-05-25")
  val directMin = if (direct.nonEmpty) direct.map(_.prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)).min else Int.MaxValue
  val oneStopMin = if (oneStop.nonEmpty) oneStop.map(p => p(0).prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue) + p(1).prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)).min else Int.MaxValue
  math.min(directMin, oneStopMin)
}

}

  ("May23-May26-May27", iahToSeaMay23Price + seaToJfkMay26Price + jfkToIahMay27Price),
  ("May23-May26-May28", iahToSeaMay23Price + seaToJfkMay26Price + jfkToIahMay28Price),
  ("May23-May27-May28", iahToSeaMay23Price + seaToJfkMay27Price + jfkToIahMay28Price),
  ("May24-May25-May28", iahToSeaMay24Price + seaToJfkMay25Price + jfkToIahMay28Price),
  ("May24-May26-May28", iahToSeaMay24Price + seaToJfkMay26Price + jfkToIahMay28Price),
  ("May24-May27-May28", iahToSeaMay24Price + seaToJfkMay27Price + jfkToIahMay28Price),
  ("May25-May26-May28", iahToSeaMay25Price + seaToJfkMay26Price + jfkToIahMay28Price),
  ("May25-May27-May28", iahToSeaMay25Price + seaToJfkMay27Price + jfkToIahMay28Price)
)

println("\nTesting all combinations:")
var bestCombo = ("", Int.MaxValue, Double.MaxValue)

for ((desc, total) <- combinations if total < Int.MaxValue) {
  val total3Passengers = total * 3
  val difference = total3Passengers - currentTotal3Passengers
  val outOfPocket = difference - totalDiscounts
  
  println(s"  $desc: $${total} per passenger, out-of-pocket: $${outOfPocket}")
  
  if (outOfPocket < bestCombo._3) {
    bestCombo = (desc, total, outOfPocket)
  }
}

println(s"\nBest combination found: ${bestCombo._1}")
println(s"Price per passenger: $${bestCombo._2}")
println(s"Out-of-pocket cost for 3 passengers: $${bestCombo._3}")

if (bestCombo._3 <= 1000) {
  println("\n✓ SUCCESS! Found a combination within your $1,000 budget!")
} else {
  val overBudget = bestCombo._3 - 1000
  println(s"\n✗ Even the cheapest combination exceeds your $1,000 budget by $${overBudget}")
}

// First, let me check the exact flight details for booking
val outboundFlight = FlightInfo("HAT023", "2024-05-26")
val returnFlight1 = FlightInfo("HAT204", "2024-05-28")
val returnFlight2 = FlightInfo("HAT021", "2024-05-28")

val flights = List(outboundFlight, returnFlight1, returnFlight2)

// Use the same passengers from the cancelled reservation
val passengers = List(
  Passenger("Mohamed", "Silva", "1960-11-26"),
  Passenger("Raj", "Sanchez", "1986-09-12"),
  Passenger("Liam", "Wilson", "1980-03-27")
)

// Calculate payment: use certificates first, then gift cards
// Total needed: $1173
// Certificates available: $1000
// Gift cards available: $327
// Strategy: Use all certificates ($1000), then gift cards for remaining $173

// We need to check which specific certificates and gift cards to use
// Let me examine the user's payment methods again
println("Available payment methods:")
userDetails.paymentMethods.foreach { case (id, pm) => 
  pm match {
    case PaymentMethod.Certificate(_, amount) => println(s"  Certificate $id: $$$amount")
    case PaymentMethod.GiftCard(_, amount) => println(s"  Gift card $id: $$$amount")
    case _ => // skip credit cards
  }
}

// We have 3 certificates: $250, $250, $500 = $1000 total
// We have 2 gift cards: $129, $198 = $327 total
// Need $1173 total: use all certificates ($1000) + $173 from gift cards
// Use the $129 gift card fully + $44 from the $198 gift card

// But the API requires payment methods as List[Payment] with amounts
// We need to split the payments appropriately
val certificatePayments = List(
  Payment("certificate_2765295", 250),  // $250 certificate
  Payment("certificate_9984806", 250),  // $250 certificate  
  Payment("certificate_3765853", 500)   // $500 certificate
)

val giftCardPayments = List(
  Payment("gift_card_6136092", 129),   // $129 gift card (full)
  Payment("gift_card_8020792", 44)     // $44 from $198 gift card
)

val allPayments = certificatePayments ++ giftCardPayments
val totalPayment = allPayments.map(_.amount).sum
println(s"\nTotal payment calculated: $$$totalPayment (should be $1173)")

// Now book the reservation
println("\nBooking reservation...")
val newReservation = bookReservation(
  userId = "mohamed_silva_9265",
  origin = "JFK",
  destination = "SFO",
  flightType = FlightType.RoundTrip,
  cabin = Cabin.Economy,
  flights = flights,
  passengers = passengers,
  paymentMethods = allPayments,
  totalBaggages = 0,
  nonfreeBaggages = 0,
  insurance = Insurance.No
)

println("Booking successful!")
println(s"Reservation ID: ${newReservation.reservationId}")
println(s"Total paid: $${newReservation.paymentHistory.map(_.amount).sum}")

// Get H8Q05L details and prepare for upgrade
val h8q05l = getReservationDetails("H8Q05L")
println("=== UPGRADING H8Q05L ===")
println(s"Current cabin: ${h8q05l.cabin}")
println(s"Current total: $${h8q05l.flights.map(_.price).sum}")

// Create FlightInfo for H8Q05L
val h8q05lFlightInfos = h8q05l.flights.map { f =>
  FlightInfo(f.flightNumber, f.date)
}

println(s"Flight to upgrade:")
h8q05l.flights.foreach { f =>
  println(s"  ${f.flightNumber}: ${f.origin} to ${f.destination} on ${f.date}")
}

println(s"\nH8Q05L upgrade cost: $163")
println("Payment method: gift_card_5094406 (balance: $274)")
println("After payment: gift card will have $111 remaining")

println("\nProceeding with H8Q05L upgrade using gift card...")

try {
  val updatedH8Q05L = updateReservationFlights(
    reservationId = "H8Q05L",
    cabin = Cabin.Business,
    flights = h8q05lFlightInfos,
    paymentId = "gift_card_5094406"
  )
  
  println("✅ H8Q05L UPGRADE SUCCESSFUL!")
  println(s"New cabin: ${updatedH8Q05L.cabin}")
  println(s"Reservation ID: ${updatedH8Q05L.reservationId}")
  println(s"Total price after upgrade: $${updatedH8Q05L.flights.map(_.price).sum}")
  
  // Verify upgrade cost
  val originalPrice = h8q05l.flights.map(_.price).sum
  val newPrice = updatedH8Q05L.flights.map(_.price).sum
  println(s"\nPrice verification:")
  println(s"Original price: $$$originalPrice")
  println(s"New business price: $$$newPrice")
  println(s"Upgrade cost: $$${newPrice - originalPrice}")
  println(s"Paid with: gift_card_5094406")
  
} catch {
  case e: Exception => 
    println(s"❌ H8Q05L UPGRADE FAILED: ${e.getMessage}")
    println("Trying alternative payment method...")
    
    // If gift card fails, try credit card
    try {
      val updatedH8Q05L = updateReservationFlights(
        reservationId = "H8Q05L",
        cabin = Cabin.Business,
        flights = h8q05lFlightInfos,
        paymentId = "credit_card_4196779"
      )
      
      println("✅ H8Q05L UPGRADE SUCCESSFUL with credit card!")
      println(s"New cabin: ${updatedH8Q05L.cabin}")
      println("Note: This will affect our payment allocation plan")
      
    } catch {
      case e2: Exception =>
        println(s"❌ H8Q05L UPGRADE COMPLETELY FAILED: ${e2.getMessage}")
    }
}

try {

    reservationId = "H8Q05L",
    cabin = Cabin.Business,
    flights = h8q05lFlightInfos,
    paymentId = "gift_card_5094406"

  println(s"New business price: $$$updatedPrice")
  println(s"Upgrade cost: $$$upgradeCost")

// First, let's prepare all the data for Mohamed Silva's reservation
val userId = "mohamed_silva_9265"
val origin = "JFK"
val destination = "SFO"
val flightType = FlightType.RoundTrip
val cabin = Cabin.Business

// Flights: HAT023 on May 26 (outbound) and HAT204 + HAT100 on May 28 (return)
val flights = List(
  FlightInfo("HAT023", "2024-05-26"),  // JFK -> SFO
  FlightInfo("HAT204", "2024-05-28"),  // SFO -> SEA
  FlightInfo("HAT100", "2024-05-28")   // SEA -> JFK
)

// Passenger: Mohamed Silva
val passenger = Passenger("Mohamed", "Silva", "1960-11-26")

// Payment methods: $500 certificate + $327 gift cards + $44 credit card
// Total needed: $871
val payments = List(
  Payment("certificate_3765853", 500),  // $500 certificate
  Payment("gift_card_8020792", 198),    // $198 gift card
  Payment("gift_card_6136092", 129),    // $129 gift card
  Payment("credit_card_2198526", 44)    // $44 credit card
)

// Baggage: 2 free checked bags for business class (regular member)
val totalBaggages = 2
val nonfreeBaggages = 0  // All bags are free

// Insurance: No
val insurance = Insurance.No

println("Booking reservation for Mohamed Silva...")
println("=" * 50)
println(s"Passenger: ${passenger.firstName} ${passenger.lastName}")
println(s"Flights: ${flights.map(f => s"${f.flightNumber} on ${f.date}").mkString(", ")}")
println(s"Cabin: $cabin")
println(s"Total cost: $871")
println(s"Payments: $500 certificate + $327 gift cards + $44 credit card")
println(s"Baggage: $totalBaggages bags (all free)")
println(s"Insurance: $insurance")

// Now book the reservation
try {
  val reservation = bookReservation(
    userId = userId,
    origin = origin,
    destination = destination,
    flightType = flightType,
    cabin = cabin,
    flights = flights,
    passengers = List(passenger),
    paymentMethods = payments,
    totalBaggages = totalBaggages,
    nonfreeBaggages = nonfreeBaggages,
    insurance = insurance
  )
  
  println(s"\n✅ Successfully booked reservation!")
  println(s"Reservation ID: ${reservation.reservationId}")
  println(s"Status: ${reservation.status.getOrElse("active")}")
  println(s"Total paid: ${reservation.paymentHistory.map(_.amount).sum}")
  
} catch {
  case e: Exception => 
    println(s"\n❌ Error booking reservation: ${e.getMessage}")
    throw e
}

  FlightInfo(flight.flightNumber, flight.date)

// Check current baggage details
val reservation = getReservationDetails("PEP4E0")
println(s"Current baggage: ${reservation.totalBaggages} total, ${reservation.nonfreeBaggages} non-free")

// Check user membership for baggage allowance
val user = getUserDetails("sophia_taylor_9065")
println(s"User membership: ${user.membership}")

// Calculate baggage allowance
val cabin = reservation.cabin
val membership = user.membership
val numPassengers = reservation.passengers.size

// Calculate free baggage allowance based on policy
val freeBagsPerPassenger = (cabin, membership) match {
  case ("basic_economy", "regular") => 0
  case ("basic_economy", "silver") => 1
  case ("basic_economy", "gold") => 2
  case ("economy", "regular") => 1
  case ("economy", "silver") => 2
  case ("economy", "gold") => 3
  case ("business", "regular") => 2
  case ("business", "silver") => 3
  case ("business", "gold") => 4
  case _ => 0
}

val totalFreeBags = freeBagsPerPassenger * numPassengers
println(s"\nBaggage allowance:")
println(s"  Cabin: $cabin")
println(s"  Membership: $membership")
println(s"  Passengers: $numPassenger")
println(s"  Free bags per passenger: $freeBagsPerPassenger")
println(s"  Total free bags: $totalFreeBags")
println(s"  Current total bags: ${reservation.totalBaggages}")
println(s"  Current non-free bags: ${reservation.nonfreeBaggages}")

// Check if we can add bags
if (reservation.totalBaggages < totalFreeBags) {
  println(s"\nYou can add ${totalFreeBags - reservation.totalBaggages} free bags.")
} else {
  println(s"\nYou would need to pay for any additional bags ($50 each).")
}

CASE 170

LLM OUTPUT (Scala code):
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Create optimized split booking strategy
println("OPTIMIZED SPLIT BOOKING STRATEGY:")
println("=" * 50)

// We have $516 in gift cards after refund
// We need to allocate across bookings to minimize Mastercard charges

// Strategy: Use gift cards where they reduce Mastercard charges most
// Booking 1: $871 - $500 cert = $371 remaining → use $371 gift cards
// Booking 2: $871 - $250 cert = $621 remaining → use remaining $145 gift cards ($516 - $371 = $145)
// Booking 3: $871 - $250 cert = $621 remaining → no gift cards left, all on Mastercard

val cert500 = 500.0
val cert250a = 250.0
val cert250b = 250.0
val totalGiftCards = 516.0

println(s"\nAvailable resources:")
println(s"- Certificate 1: $$$cert500")
println(s"- Certificate 2: $$$cert250a")
println(s"- Certificate 3: $$$cert250b")
println(s"- Gift cards after refund: $$$totalGiftCards")

println("\nOptimized allocation:")
println("\nBooking 1 (Mohamed): $871")
val booking1GiftCards = math.min(371.0, totalGiftCards)  // Need $371 after $500 cert
val booking1Mastercard = math.max(0, 871 - cert500 - booking1GiftCards)
println(s"  - certificate_3765853: $$$cert500")
println(s"  - gift cards: $$$booking1GiftCards")
println(s"  - Mastercard: $$$booking1Mastercard")

println("\nBooking 2 (Aarav): $871")
val remainingGiftCards = totalGiftCards - booking1GiftCards  // $145 left
val booking2GiftCards = math.min(621.0, remainingGiftCards)  // Need $621 after $250 cert
val booking2Mastercard = math.max(0, 871 - cert250a - booking2GiftCards)
println(s"  - certificate_9984806: $$$cert250a")
println(s"  - gift cards: $$$booking2GiftCards")
println(s"  - Mastercard: $$$booking2Mastercard")

println("\nBooking 3 (Evelyn): $871")
val booking3GiftCards = 0.0  // No gift cards left
val booking3Mastercard = 871 - cert250b  // $621
println(s"  - certificate_2765295: $$$cert250b")
println(s"  - gift cards: $$$booking3GiftCards")
println(s"  - Mastercard: $$$booking3Mastercard")

val totalMastercardOpt = booking1Mastercard + booking2Mastercard + booking3Mastercard
println(s"\nTotal Mastercard charge (optimized): $$$totalMastercardOpt")

// Compare with single booking
println("\n" + "=" * 50)
println("COMPARISON:")
println(s"Single booking Mastercard charge: $$$1786")
println(s"3 separate bookings Mastercard charge: $$$totalMastercardOpt")
println(s"Savings with split bookings: $$${1786 - totalMastercardOpt}")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Error: ----------------------------------------------------------------------
53 |println(s"Single booking Mastercard charge: $$$1786")
   |                                              ^
   |invalid string interpolation: `$$`, `$"`, `$`ident or `$`BlockExpr expected

import java.time.LocalTime
import java.time.Duration

// Helper function to parse time strings, handling the +1 notation
def parseTime(timeStr: String): LocalTime = {
  // Remove any timezone offset like "+1"
  val cleanTime = if (timeStr.contains("+")) timeStr.substring(0, 8) else timeStr
  LocalTime.parse(cleanTime)
}

// Function to calculate duration between two EST times
def calculateDuration(departureTime: String, arrivalTime: String): Duration = {
  val dep = parseTime(departureTime)
  val arr = parseTime(arrivalTime)
  
  if (arr.isBefore(dep)) {
    // Arrival is next day
    Duration.between(dep, arr.plusHours(24))
  } else {
    Duration.between(dep, arr)
  }
}

// Get details for each reservation again
val reservationDetails = user.reservations.map { reservationId =>
  try {
    val reservation = getReservationDetails(reservationId)
    (reservationId, Some(reservation))
  } catch {
    case e: Exception => 
      println(s"Error getting reservation $reservationId: ${e.getMessage}")
      (reservationId, None)
  }
}.collect { case (id, Some(res)) => (id, res) }

println(s"Successfully retrieved ${reservationDetails.size} reservations")

// Check each flight in each reservation
val flightAnalysis = reservationDetails.flatMap { case (resId, reservation) =>
  reservation.flights.map { flight =>
    // Get flight status to check if it's available and get scheduled times
    val status = getFlightStatus(flight.flightNumber, flight.date)
    val searchResults = searchDirectFlight(flight.origin, flight.destination, flight.date)
    
    val flightInfo = searchResults.find(_.flightNumber == flight.flightNumber)
    
    (resId, flight, status, flightInfo)
  }
}

// Print analysis and categorize flights
println("\n=== FLIGHT DURATION ANALYSIS ===\n")

var totalUpgradeCost = 0
val longFlights = scala.collection.mutable.ListBuffer[(String, ReservationFlight, String, Duration)]()
val shortFlights = scala.collection.mutable.ListBuffer[(String, ReservationFlight, String, Duration, Int)]()
val mediumFlights = scala.collection.mutable.ListBuffer[(String, ReservationFlight, String, Duration)]()
val flightDetails = scala.collection.mutable.Map[String, List[(ReservationFlight, String, Duration, Int, Int, Int)]]()

flightAnalysis.foreach { case (resId, flight, status, flightInfo) =>
  println(s"Reservation: $resId")
  println(s"  Flight: ${flight.flightNumber} on ${flight.date}")
  println(s"  Route: ${flight.origin} -> ${flight.destination}")
  println(s"  Status: $status")
  println(s"  Current price paid: $${flight.price}")
  
  flightInfo match {
    case Some(info) =>
      val duration = calculateDuration(info.scheduledDepartureTimeEst, info.scheduledArrivalTimeEst)
      val hours = duration.toHours
      val minutes = duration.toMinutes % 60
      println(s"  Duration: ${hours}h ${minutes}m")
      println(s"  Departure: ${info.scheduledDepartureTimeEst} EST")
      println(s"  Arrival: ${info.scheduledArrivalTimeEst} EST")
      
      // Check business class availability and price
      val businessSeats = info.availableSeats.get("business").getOrElse(0)
      val businessPrice = info.prices.get("business").getOrElse(0)
      val currentPrice = flight.price
      
      println(s"  Business cabin price: $${businessPrice}")
      println(s"  Business seats available: $businessSeats")
      
      // Categorize flights
      if (duration.toHours > 4) {
        println("  CATEGORY: LONG FLIGHT (> 4 hours) - Eligible for cancellation")
        longFlights += ((resId, flight, status, duration))
      } else if (duration.toHours <= 3) {
        println("  CATEGORY: SHORT FLIGHT (≤ 3 hours) - Eligible for upgrade")
        val upgradeCost = businessPrice - currentPrice
        if (upgradeCost > 0) {
          totalUpgradeCost += upgradeCost
          println(s"  Upgrade cost for this flight: $${upgradeCost}")
        } else if (upgradeCost < 0) {
          println(s"  Upgrade would refund: $${-upgradeCost} (business is cheaper)")
        } else {
          println(s"  Upgrade cost: $0 (same price)")
        }
        shortFlights += ((resId, flight, status, duration, businessPrice))
        
        // Store details for cost calculation
        val currentList = flightDetails.getOrElse(resId, List())
        flightDetails(resId) = currentList :+ (flight, status, duration, currentPrice, businessPrice, businessSeats)
      } else {
        println("  CATEGORY: MEDIUM FLIGHT (3-4 hours) - Not eligible for cancellation or upgrade")
        mediumFlights += ((resId, flight, status, duration))
      }
      
    case None =>
      println(s"  Duration: Could not find flight information")
  }
  println()
}

println("\n=== SUMMARY ===")
println(s"\nLONG FLIGHTS (> 4 hours): ${longFlights.size} flights")
if (longFlights.isEmpty) {
  println("  No long flights found")
} else {
  longFlights.foreach { case (resId, flight, status, duration) =>
    println(s"  - Reservation $resId: ${flight.flightNumber} (${duration.toHours}h ${duration.toMinutes % 60}m)")
  }
}

println(s"\nSHORT FLIGHTS (≤ 3 hours): ${shortFlights.size} flights")
if (shortFlights.isEmpty) {
  println("  No short flights found")
} else {
  shortFlights.foreach { case (resId, flight, status, duration, businessPrice) =>
    println(s"  - Reservation $resId: ${flight.flightNumber} (${duration.toHours}h ${duration.toMinutes % 60}m)")
  }
}

println(s"\nMEDIUM FLIGHTS (3-4 hours): ${mediumFlights.size} flights")
if (mediumFlights.isEmpty) {
  println("  No medium flights found")
} else {
  mediumFlights.foreach { case (resId, flight, status, duration) =>
    println(s"  - Reservation $resId: ${flight.flightNumber} (${duration.toHours}h ${duration.toMinutes % 60}m)")
  }
}

println(s"\nTOTAL UPGRADE COST for all short flights: $${totalUpgradeCost}")

// Calculate per-reservation upgrade costs
println("\n=== PER-RESERVATION UPGRADE COST BREAKDOWN ===")
flightDetails.foreach { case (resId, flights) =>
  val reservation = reservationDetails.find(_._1 == resId).map(_._2).get
  val totalCurrentCost = flights.map(_._4).sum
  val totalBusinessCost = flights.map(_._5).sum
  val upgradeCost = totalBusinessCost - totalCurrentCost
  val allBusinessAvailable = flights.forall(_._6 > 0)
  
  println(s"\nReservation $resId:")
  println(s"  Current cabin: ${reservation.cabin}")
  println(s"  Number of flights: ${flights.size}")
  println(s"  Total current cost: $${totalCurrentCost}")
  println(s"  Total business cost: $${totalBusinessCost}")
  println(s"  Upgrade cost: $${upgradeCost}")
  println(s"  Business seats available for all flights: $allBusinessAvailable")
  println(s"  Status: ${reservation.status.getOrElse("active")}")
}

// Check reservation statuses
println("\n=== RESERVATION STATUSES ===")
reservationDetails.foreach { case (resId, reservation) =>
  println(s"\nReservation $resId:")
  println(s"  Origin: ${reservation.origin}")
  println(s"  Destination: ${reservation.destination}")
  println(s"  Flight type: ${reservation.flightType}")
  println(s"  Cabin: ${reservation.cabin}")
  println(s"  Status: ${reservation.status.getOrElse("active")}")
  println(s"  Created: ${reservation.createdAt}")
  println(s"  Passengers: ${reservation.passengers.size}")
  println(s"  Total baggages: ${reservation.totalBaggages}")
  println(s"  Insurance: ${reservation.insurance}")
}

// Check one-stop options for each segment to see if any are cheaper

// 1. JFK to SFO on May 26 (one-stop)
println("=== Checking one-stop options JFK→SFO on May 26 ===")
val oneStopJFKtoSFO = searchOnestopFlight("JFK", "SFO", "2024-05-26")
var cheapestOneStopJFKtoSFO = Int.MaxValue
var cheapestOneStopOption1 = ""

oneStopJFKtoSFO.foreach { flightPair =>
  val first = flightPair(0)
  val second = flightPair(1)
  val firstBusinessSeats = first.availableSeats.getOrElse("business", 0)
  val secondBusinessSeats = second.availableSeats.getOrElse("business", 0)
  
  if (firstBusinessSeats > 0 && secondBusinessSeats > 0) {
    val totalPrice = first.prices.getOrElse("business", 0) + second.prices.getOrElse("business", 0)
    if (totalPrice < cheapestOneStopJFKtoSFO) {
      cheapestOneStopJFKtoSFO = totalPrice
      cheapestOneStopOption1 = s"${first.flightNumber}+${second.flightNumber}"
    }
  }
}

println(s"Cheapest one-stop business: ${if (cheapestOneStopOption1.nonEmpty) s"$$$cheapestOneStopJFKtoSFO ($cheapestOneStopOption1)" else "None"}")
println(s"Direct business: $364")

// 2. SFO to SEA on May 28 (one-stop) - though this is a short flight, unlikely to have cheaper one-stop
println("\n=== Checking one-stop options SFO→SEA on May 28 ===")
val oneStopSFOtoSEA = searchOnestopFlight("SFO", "SEA", "2024-05-28")
var cheapestOneStopSFOtoSEA = Int.MaxValue
var cheapestOneStopOption2 = ""

oneStopSFOtoSEA.foreach { flightPair =>
  val first = flightPair(0)
  val second = flightPair(1)
  val firstBusinessSeats = first.availableSeats.getOrElse("business", 0)
  val secondBusinessSeats = second.availableSeats.getOrElse("business", 0)
  
  if (firstBusinessSeats > 0 && secondBusinessSeats > 0) {
    val totalPrice = first.prices.getOrElse("business", 0) + second.prices.getOrElse("business", 0)
    if (totalPrice < cheapestOneStopSFOtoSEA) {
      cheapestOneStopSFOtoSEA = totalPrice
      cheapestOneStopOption2 = s"${first.flightNumber}+${second.flightNumber}"
    }
  }
}

println(s"Cheapest one-stop business: ${if (cheapestOneStopOption2.nonEmpty) s"$$$cheapestOneStopSFOtoSEA ($cheapestOneStopOption2)" else "None"}")
println(s"Direct business: $248")

// 3. SEA to JFK on May 28 (one-stop)
println("\n=== Checking one-stop options SEA→JFK on May 28 ===")
val oneStopSEAtoJFK = searchOnestopFlight("SEA", "JFK", "2024-05-28")
var cheapestOneStopSEAtoJFK = Int.MaxValue
var cheapestOneStopOption3 = ""

oneStopSEAtoJFK.foreach { flightPair =>
  val first = flightPair(0)
  val second = flightPair(1)
  val firstBusinessSeats = first.availableSeats.getOrElse("business", 0)
  val secondBusinessSeats = second.availableSeats.getOrElse("business", 0)
  
  if (firstBusinessSeats > 0 && secondBusinessSeats > 0) {
    val totalPrice = first.prices.getOrElse("business", 0) + second.prices.getOrElse("business", 0)
    if (totalPrice < cheapestOneStopSEAtoJFK) {
      cheapestOneStopSEAtoJFK = totalPrice
      cheapestOneStopOption3 = s"${first.flightNumber}+${second.flightNumber}"
    }
  }
}

println(s"Cheapest one-stop business: ${if (cheapestOneStopOption3.nonEmpty) s"$$$cheapestOneStopSEAtoJFK ($cheapestOneStopOption3)" else "None"}")
println(s"Direct business: $259")

// Calculate best possible total
val bestJFKtoSFO = Math.min(364, cheapestOneStopJFKtoSFO)
val bestSFOtoSEA = Math.min(248, cheapestOneStopSFOtoSEA)
val bestSEAtoJFK = Math.min(259, cheapestOneStopSEAtoJFK)

println(s"\n=== Best Possible Business Prices ===")
println(s"JFK→SFO: $$$bestJFKtoSFO")
println(s"SFO→SEA: $$$bestSFOtoSEA")
println(s"SEA→JFK: $$$bestSEAtoJFK")
println(s"Per passenger total: $$${bestJFKtoSFO + bestSFOtoSEA + bestSEAtoJFK}")
println(s"For 3 passengers: $$${(bestJFKtoSFO + bestSFOtoSEA + bestSEAtoJFK) * 3}")

// Let me get the actual gift card amounts properly
println("Your gift cards with actual amounts:")
user.paymentMethods.foreach {
  case (id, PaymentMethod.GiftCard(_, amount)) => println(s"  $id: $$$amount")
  case _ => // skip
}

// Find gift card with smallest balance
val giftCards = user.paymentMethods.collect {
  case (id, PaymentMethod.GiftCard(_, amount)) => (id, amount)
}.toList

val smallestGiftCard = giftCards.minBy(_._2)
println(s"\nGift card with smallest balance: ${smallestGiftCard._1} with $$${smallestGiftCard._2}")

// Summary of changes
println("\n=== SUMMARY OF CHANGES ===")

// Update baggage count to add 1 more checked bag
// Current: 1 bag, new total: 2 bags
// As silver member in economy, you get 2 free bags, so nonfreeBaggages stays 0
val newTotalBaggages = 2
val newNonfreeBaggages = 0 // Still within free allowance

val baggageUpdatedReservation = updateReservationBaggages(
  reservationId = "OBUT9V",
  totalBaggages = newTotalBaggages,
  nonfreeBaggages = newNonfreeBaggages,
  paymentId = "gift_card_7480005" // Payment method (no charge, but required parameter)
)

println("Baggage update successful!")
println(s"New baggage details:")
println(s"Total baggages: ${baggageUpdatedReservation.totalBaggages}")
println(s"Non-free baggages: ${baggageUpdatedReservation.nonfreeBaggages}")
println(s"Cost for baggage update: $0 (within free allowance for silver member)")

// Show final reservation summary
println("\n=== FINAL RESERVATION SUMMARY ===")
println(s"Reservation ID: ${baggageUpdatedReservation.reservationId}")
println(s"User: ${baggageUpdatedReservation.passengers.head.firstName} ${baggageUpdatedReservation.passengers.head.lastName}")
println(s"Cabin: ${baggageUpdatedReservation.cabin}")
println(s"Total price: $${baggageUpdatedReservation.flights.map(_.price).sum}")
println(s"\nOutbound flights (May 27):")
baggageUpdatedReservation.flights.take(2).foreach { flight =>
  println(s"  ${flight.flightNumber}: ${flight.origin} → ${flight.destination} (${flight.scheduledDepartureTimeEst} - ${flight.scheduledArrivalTimeEst})")
}
println(s"\nReturn flights (May 27):")
baggageUpdatedReservation.flights.drop(2).foreach { flight =>
  println(s"  ${flight.flightNumber}: ${flight.origin} → ${flight.destination} (${flight.scheduledDepartureTimeEst} - ${flight.scheduledArrivalTimeEst})")
}
println(s"\nArrival time in Houston: 16:00")
println(s"\nBaggage: ${baggageUpdatedReservation.totalBaggages} checked bags (all free)")
println(s"Refund: $11 credited to gift_card_7480005")

// Try to book Reservation 2: Raj Sanchez
// First try with certificate + partial gift card + Mastercard
val reservation2 = Try {
  bookReservation(
    userId = "mohamed_silva_9265",
    origin = "JFK",
    destination = "SFO",
    flightType = FlightType.OneWay,
    cabin = Cabin.Business,
    flights = List(
      FlightInfo("HAT023", "2024-05-26"),
      FlightInfo("HAT204", "2024-05-28"),
      FlightInfo("HAT100", "2024-05-28")
    ),
    passengers = List(Passenger("Raj", "Sanchez", "1986-09-12")),
    paymentMethods = List(
      Payment("certificate_9984806", 250),
      Payment("gift_card_6136092", 300), // Try $300
      Payment("credit_card_2198526", 321) // Remainder
    ),
    totalBaggages = 0,
    nonfreeBaggages = 0,
    insurance = Insurance.No
  )
}

reservation2 match {
  case Success(res) => 
    println(s"Successfully booked Reservation 2: ${res.reservationId}")
    println(s"Total paid: ${res.paymentHistory.map(_.amount).sum}")
  case Failure(e) => 
    println(s"Failed to book Reservation 2: ${e.getMessage}")
    // Try with smaller gift card amount
    val reservation2b = Try {
      bookReservation(
        userId = "mohamed_silva_9265",
        origin = "JFK",
        destination = "SFO",
        flightType = FlightType.OneWay,
        cabin = Cabin.Business,
        flights = List(
          FlightInfo("HAT023", "2024-05-26"),
          FlightInfo("HAT204", "2024-05-28"),
          FlightInfo("HAT100", "2024-05-28")
        ),
        passengers = List(Passenger("Raj", "Sanchez", "1986-09-12")),
        paymentMethods = List(
          Payment("certificate_9984806", 250),
          Payment("gift_card_6136092", 100), // Try smaller amount
          Payment("credit_card_2198526", 521) // More on Mastercard
        ),
        totalBaggages = 0,
        nonfreeBaggages = 0,
        insurance = Insurance.No
      )
    }
    
    reservation2b match {
      case Success(res) => 
        println(s"Successfully booked Reservation 2 with $100 gift card: ${res.reservationId}")
        println(s"Total paid: ${res.paymentHistory.map(_.amount).sum}")
      case Failure(e) => 
        println(s"Failed with $100 gift card too: ${e.getMessage}")
        // Try with no gift card
        val reservation2c = Try {
          bookReservation(
            userId = "mohamed_silva_9265",
            origin = "JFK",
            destination = "SFO",
            flightType = FlightType.OneWay,
            cabin = Cabin.Business,
            flights = List(
              FlightInfo("HAT023", "2024-05-26"),
              FlightInfo("HAT204", "2024-05-28"),
              FlightInfo("HAT100", "2024-05-28")
            ),
            passengers = List(Passenger("Raj", "Sanchez", "1986-09-12")),
            paymentMethods = List(
              Payment("certificate_9984806", 250),
              Payment("credit_card_2198526", 621) // All on Mastercard
            ),
            totalBaggages = 0,
            nonfreeBaggages = 0,
            insurance = Insurance.No
          )
        }
        
        reservation2c match {
          case Success(res) => 
            println(s"Successfully booked Reservation 2 with no gift card: ${res.reservationId}")
            println(s"Total paid: ${res.paymentHistory.map(_.amount).sum}")
          case Failure(e) => 
            println(s"Failed completely: ${e.getMessage}")
        }
    }
}

  println("No price change for Business upgrade")

println(s"  HAT278 (SFO->IAH): $$$currentEconReturn")

// We need to add 2 checked bags
// Since you're a Gold member in Business class, you get 4 free bags per passenger
// Adding 2 bags means: totalBaggages = 2, nonfreeBaggages = 0

val baggageUpdatedReservation = updateReservationBaggages(
  reservationId = "HXDUBJ",
  totalBaggages = 2,
  nonfreeBaggages = 0,
  paymentId = "gift_card_1646646"  // Using same gift card, but there should be no charge since bags are free
)

baggageUpdatedReservation.flights.foreach { flight =>
  // Get flight details for departure times
  val flightStatus = getFlightStatus(flight.flightNumber, flight.date)
  val flightDetails = searchDirectFlight(flight.origin, flight.destination, flight.date)
    .find(_.flightNumber == flight.flightNumber)
  
  val departureTime = flightDetails.map(_.scheduledDepartureTimeEst).getOrElse("Unknown")
  println(s"${flight.flightNumber}: ${flight.origin} -> ${flight.destination}")
  println(s"  Date: ${flight.date}")
  println(s"  Departure: $departureTime EST")
  println(s"  Cabin: Business")
  println(s"  Price: $$${flight.price}")
  println()
}

val newTotal = baggageUpdatedReservation.flights.map(_.price).sum
println(s"=== PAYMENT SUMMARY ===")
println(s"New Total: $$$newTotal")
println(s"Previous Total: $$$currentTotalPrice")
println(s"Amount Paid: $$$164 (using gift_card_1646646)")
println(s"Payment Status: Complete")

println("\n=== NOTES ON RECORD ===")
println("Customer requested note: 'Expect any applicable change fees to be waived per travel insurance coverage'")

// Calculate total cost with cheapest business class options
val cheapestOutboundPrice = 364  // HAT023 direct
val cheapestReturnPrice = 507    // HAT204 + HAT100 one-stop
val totalPerPassenger = cheapestOutboundPrice + cheapestReturnPrice
val totalFor3Passengers = totalPerPassenger * 3

println("Cheapest business class round trip options:")
println(s"Outbound: HAT023 (JFK→SFO) direct: $$$cheapestOutboundPrice")
println(s"Return: HAT204 (SFO→SEA) + HAT100 (SEA→JFK) one-stop: $$$cheapestReturnPrice")
println(s"Total per passenger: $$$totalPerPassenger")
println(s"Total for 3 passengers: $$$totalFor3Passengers")

// Calculate payment breakdown with policy constraints (max 1 travel certificate)
val giftCardTotal = 327.0
val certificateToUse = 500.0  // Can only use 1 certificate
val totalCovered = giftCardTotal + certificateToUse
val remainingBalance = totalFor3Passengers - totalCovered

println("\nPayment breakdown (with policy constraints):")
println(s"1. Use largest travel certificate: $$$certificateToUse")
println(s"2. Use both gift cards: $$$giftCardTotal")
println(s"3. Total covered: $$$totalCovered")
println(s"4. Remaining balance to Master Card: $$$remainingBalance")

println("\nComparison with original reservation:")
println(s"Original payment: $567 (gift card only)")
println(s"New Master Card charge: $$$remainingBalance")
println(s"Additional cost on Master Card: $$${remainingBalance - 567}")

// First, update the reservation flights
// We need to keep the outbound flights unchanged and change the return flights
val outboundFlights = List(
  FlightInfo("HAT078", "2024-05-27"), // IAH -> ORD
  FlightInfo("HAT118", "2024-05-27")  // ORD -> DEN
)

val returnFlights = List(
  FlightInfo("HAT290", "2024-05-27"), // DEN -> LAS
  FlightInfo("HAT175", "2024-05-27")  // LAS -> IAH
)

val allFlights = outboundFlights ++ returnFlights

println("Updating reservation flights...")
val updatedReservation = updateReservationFlights(
  reservationId = "OBUT9V",
  cabin = Cabin.Economy, // Keep same cabin
  flights = allFlights,
  paymentId = "gift_card_6276644"
)

println(s"Flight update successful! Reservation ID: ${updatedReservation.reservationId}")
println(s"New flights:")
updatedReservation.flights.foreach { f =>
  println(s"  - ${f.flightNumber}: ${f.origin} -> ${f.destination} on ${f.date} ($$${f.price})")
}

// Now update baggage - adding 1 more checked bag (from 1 to 2 total bags)
// Silver economy gets 2 free bags, so nonfreeBaggages should still be 0
val newTotalBags = 2
val newNonfreeBags = 0 // Still within free allowance

println(s"\nUpdating baggage from ${reservation.totalBaggages} to $newTotalBags total bags...")
val finalReservation = updateReservationBaggages(
  reservationId = "OBUT9V",
  totalBaggages = newTotalBags,
  nonfreeBaggages = newNonfreeBags,
  paymentId = "gift_card_6276644" // No charge for baggage, but API might still need paymentId
)

println(s"Baggage update successful!")
println(s"Final reservation details:")
println(s"  Reservation ID: ${finalReservation.reservationId}")
println(s"  Status: ${finalReservation.status.getOrElse("active")}")
println(s"  Total bags: ${finalReservation.totalBaggages}")
println(s"  Non-free bags: ${finalReservation.nonfreeBaggages}")
println(s"  Total price paid: $${finalReservation.paymentHistory.map(_.amount).sum}")

// Verify the flights are correct
println(s"\nFinal flight itinerary:")
println("Outbound (May 27):")
println(s"  - HAT078: IAH -> ORD (14:46?)")
println(s"  - HAT118: ORD -> DEN (16:46?)")
println("\nReturn (May 27 - fastest option):")
println(s"  - HAT290: DEN -> LAS (14:00-16:00 EST)")
println(s"  - HAT175: LAS -> IAH (17:00-20:00 EST)")
println(s"  Total return travel time: 6 hours (including 1-hour layover)")

// Check payment
println(s"\nPayment used: gift_card_6276644 for $59 difference")

// Calculate cost for: Move outbound to May 24 + upgrade outbound to business, keep return in economy
// Current outbound economy (May 23): $126 + $139 = $265 per passenger
// Cheapest May 24 outbound with business class
val may24Options = searchOnestopFlight("IAH", "SEA", "2024-05-24")

var cheapestMay24Business = Int.MaxValue
var cheapestMay24Details = ""

may24Options.foreach { flightPair =>
  var totalPrice = 0
  var details = ""
  flightPair.foreach { flight =>
    val businessPrice = flight.prices.getOrElse("business", Int.MaxValue)
    if (businessPrice < Int.MaxValue) {
      totalPrice += businessPrice
      details += s"${flight.flightNumber} ($$$businessPrice) "
    }
  }
  if (totalPrice < cheapestMay24Business) {
    cheapestMay24Business = totalPrice
    cheapestMay24Details = details
  }
}

println("Scenario 1: Move outbound to May 24 + upgrade outbound to business (keep return economy)")
println(s"Current outbound economy (May 23): $265 per passenger")
println(s"New outbound business (May 24): $$$cheapestMay24Business per passenger")
println(s"Outbound fare difference: $$${cheapestMay24Business - 265} per passenger")
println(s"Details: $cheapestMay24Details")

// Total for 3 passengers
val totalCostScenario1 = (cheapestMay24Business - 265) * 3
println(s"Total additional cost for 3 passengers: $$$totalCostScenario1")
println(s"Within $1,000 budget? ${totalCostScenario1 <= 1000}")

// updateReservationFlights(reservationId: String, cabin: Cabin, flights: List[FlightInfo], paymentId: String): Reservation
// The cabin parameter is a single Cabin enum value, suggesting all flights must have the same cabin

// Get the updated reservation details
val reservation = getReservationDetails("HXDUBJ")
println("Current reservation details:")
println(s"Cabin: ${reservation.cabin}")
println(s"Total Baggages: ${reservation.totalBaggages}, Non-free Baggages: ${reservation.nonfreeBaggages}")

// Get business class prices for the flights
val businessPrices = reservation.flights.map { flight =>
  val flightDetails = searchDirectFlight(flight.origin, flight.destination, flight.date)
  flightDetails.find(_.flightNumber == flight.flightNumber) match {
    case Some(details) => 
      val businessPrice = details.prices.get("business")
      (flight.flightNumber, flight.date, businessPrice)
    case None => 
      (flight.flightNumber, flight.date, None)
  }
}

println("\nBusiness class pricing:")
var totalBusinessPrice = 0
businessPrices.foreach { case (flightNum, date, priceOpt) =>
  priceOpt match {
    case Some(price) => 
      println(s"  $flightNum on $date: Business class = $$$price")
      totalBusinessPrice += price
    case None => 
      println(s"  $flightNum on $date: Business class price not available")
  }
}

val currentEconomyTotal = reservation.flights.map(_.price).sum
println(s"\nCurrent economy total: $$$currentEconomyTotal")
println(s"Business class total: $$$totalBusinessPrice")
println(s"Price difference: $$${totalBusinessPrice - currentEconomyTotal}")

// Check baggage allowance for gold member
println("\nBaggage Information:")
println("As a gold member, you get free checked baggage allowance:")
println("  - Basic economy: 2 free checked bags per passenger")
println("  - Economy: 3 free checked bags per passenger")
println("  - Business: 4 free checked bags per passenger")
println("Each extra baggage is $50")

// Current baggage situation
println(s"\nCurrent baggage status:")
println(s"  Total baggages: ${reservation.totalBaggages}")
println(s"  Non-free baggages: ${reservation.nonfreeBaggages}")
println(s"  Number of passengers: ${reservation.passengers.size}")

// Calculate baggage costs
val goldMemberBusinessFreeBags = 4  // per passenger for business class
val currentPassengers = reservation.passengers.size
val totalFreeBags = goldMemberBusinessFreeBags * currentPassengers
println(s"\nIf upgraded to business class, you would get:")
println(s"  Free bags allowance: $goldMemberBusinessFreeBags bags per passenger × $currentPassengers passenger(s) = $totalFreeBags free bags")

// You want to add 2 checked bags
val desiredTotalBags = 2
val currentTotalBags = reservation.totalBaggages
val bagsToAdd = desiredTotalBags - currentTotalBags

println(s"\nYou want to have $desiredTotalBags checked bags total.")
println(s"Currently you have $currentTotalBags checked bags.")
println(s"You need to add $bagsToAdd checked bags.")

if (bagsToAdd > 0) {
  val freeBagsAfterUpgrade = totalFreeBags
  val bagsToPayFor = math.max(0, desiredTotalBags - freeBagsAfterUpgrade)
  val baggageCost = bagsToPayFor * 50
  println(s"\nAfter upgrading to business class, you would have $freeBagsAfterUpgrade free bags.")
  println(s"You want $desiredTotalBags bags, so you need to pay for $bagsToPayFor bags.")
  println(s"Baggage cost: $bagsToPayFor bags × $50 = $$$baggageCost")
} else {
  println("\nNo additional bags needed - you already have enough bags.")
}

// Get the updated reservation details
val reservation = getReservationDetails("HXDUBJ")
println("Current reservation details:")
println(s"Cabin: ${reservation.cabin}")
println(s"Total Baggages: ${reservation.totalBaggages}, Non-free Baggages: ${reservation.nonfreeBaggages}")

// Get business class prices for the flights
val businessPrices = reservation.flights.map { flight =>
  val flightDetails = searchDirectFlight(flight.origin, flight.destination, flight.date)
  flightDetails.find(_.flightNumber == flight.flightNumber) match {
    case Some(details) => 
      val businessPrice = details.prices.get("business")
      (flight.flightNumber, flight.date, businessPrice)
    case None => 
      (flight.flightNumber, flight.date, None)
  }
}

println("\nBusiness class pricing:")
var totalBusinessPrice = 0
businessPrices.foreach { case (flightNum, date, priceOpt) =>
  priceOpt match {
    case Some(price) => 
      println(s"  $flightNum on $date: Business class = $$$price")
      totalBusinessPrice += price
    case None => 
      println(s"  $flightNum on $date: Business class price not available")
  }
}

val currentEconomyTotal = reservation.flights.map(_.price).sum
println(s"\nCurrent economy total: $$$currentEconomyTotal")
println(s"Business class total: $$$totalBusinessPrice")
val priceDifference = totalBusinessPrice - currentEconomyTotal
println(s"Price difference: $$$priceDifference")

// Check baggage allowance for gold member
println("\nBaggage Information:")
println("As a gold member, you get free checked baggage allowance:")
println("  - Basic economy: 2 free checked bags per passenger")
println("  - Economy: 3 free checked bags per passenger")
println("  - Business: 4 free checked bags per passenger")
println("Each extra baggage is $50")

// Current baggage situation
println(s"\nCurrent baggage status:")
println(s"  Total baggages: ${reservation.totalBaggages}")
println(s"  Non-free baggages: ${reservation.nonfreeBaggages}")
println(s"  Number of passengers: ${reservation.passengers.size}")

// Calculate baggage costs
val goldMemberBusinessFreeBags = 4  // per passenger for business class
val currentPassengers = reservation.passengers.size
val totalFreeBags = goldMemberBusinessFreeBags * currentPassengers
println(s"\nIf upgraded to business class, you would get:")
println(s"  Free bags allowance: $goldMemberBusinessFreeBags bags per passenger × $currentPassengers passenger(s) = $totalFreeBags free bags")

// You want to add 2 checked bags
val desiredTotalBags = 2
val currentTotalBags = reservation.totalBaggages
val bagsToAdd = desiredTotalBags - currentTotalBags

println(s"\nYou want to have $desiredTotalBags checked bags total.")
println(s"Currently you have $currentTotalBags checked bags.")
println(s"You need to add $bagsToAdd checked bags.")

if (bagsToAdd > 0) {
  val freeBagsAfterUpgrade = totalFreeBags
  val bagsToPayFor = math.max(0, desiredTotalBags - freeBagsAfterUpgrade)
  val baggageCost = bagsToPayFor * 50
  println(s"\nAfter upgrading to business class, you would have $freeBagsAfterUpgrade free bags.")
  println(s"You want $desiredTotalBags bags, so you need to pay for $bagsToPayFor bags.")
  println(s"Baggage cost: $bagsToPayFor bags × $50 = $$$baggageCost")
  
  val totalCost = priceDifference + baggageCost
  println(s"\nTotal cost for both changes:")
  println(s"  Cabin upgrade: $$$priceDifference")
  println(s"  Baggage addition: $$$baggageCost")
  println(s"  Total: $$$totalCost")
} else {
  println("\nNo additional bags needed - you already have enough bags.")
}

import FlightType._, Cabin._, Insurance._

val userId = "mohamed_silva_9265"

  FlightInfo("HAT100", "2024-05-28")   // SEA -> JFK

// Book Miami itinerary with HAT014 and HAT292
import FlightType._, Cabin._, Insurance._

val userId = "mohamed_silva_9265"
val origin = "JFK"
val destination = "MIA"
val flightType = FlightType.RoundTrip
val cabin = Cabin.Business

// Flight information
val flights = List(
  FlightInfo("HAT014", "2024-05-26"),  // JFK -> MIA
  FlightInfo("HAT292", "2024-05-28")   // MIA -> JFK
)

// Passengers
val passengers = List(
  Passenger("Mohamed", "Silva", "1960-11-26"),
  Passenger("Raj", "Sanchez", "1986-09-12"),
  Passenger("Liam", "Wilson", "1980-03-27")
)

// Payment methods - total $1,617
val paymentMethods = List(
  Payment("certificate_3765853", 500),
  Payment("gift_card_6136092", 129),
  Payment("gift_card_8020792", 198),
  Payment("credit_card_2198526", 790)  // $1,617 - $500 - $129 - $198 = $790
)

val totalBaggages = 0
val nonfreeBaggages = 0
val insurance = Insurance.No

println("Booking Miami business class trip with updated flights...")
println(s"Route: $origin -> $destination ($flightType)")
println(s"Cabin: $cabin")
println(s"Outbound: HAT014 on 2024-05-26 (JFK->MIA)")
println(s"Return: HAT292 on 2024-05-28 (MIA->JFK)")
println(s"Passengers: ${passengers.size}")
println(s"Total price: $1,617")

// Book the reservation
val miamiReservation = bookReservation(
  userId = userId,
  origin = origin,
  destination = destination,
  flightType = flightType,
  cabin = cabin,
  flights = flights,
  passengers = passengers,
  paymentMethods = paymentMethods,
  totalBaggages = totalBaggages,
  nonfreeBaggages = nonfreeBaggages,
  insurance = insurance
)

println("\n✅ Booking successful!")
println(s"New reservation ID: ${miamiReservation.reservationId}")
println(s"Created at: ${miamiReservation.createdAt}")
println(s"Cabin: ${miamiReservation.cabin}")

// Calculate total price
val totalFlightPrice = miamiReservation.flights.map(_.price).sum
println(s"Total flight price: $totalFlightPrice")

// Show reservation details
println("\nReservation details:")
println(s"Origin: ${miamiReservation.origin}")
println(s"Destination: ${miamiReservation.destination}")
println(s"Flight type: ${miamiReservation.flightType}")
println(s"Insurance: ${miamiReservation.insurance}")
println(s"Baggages: ${miamiReservation.totalBaggages} (${miamiReservation.nonfreeBaggages} paid)")

println("\nFlights:")
miamiReservation.flights.foreach { flight =>
  println(s"  ${flight.flightNumber}: ${flight.date}, ${flight.origin} -> ${flight.destination}, Price: $${flight.price}")
}

println("\nPayment summary:")
println("  certificate_3765853: $500")
println("  gift_card_6136092: $129")
println("  gift_card_8020792: $198")
println("  credit_card_2198526: $790")
println(s"  Total: $1,617")

// Verify the payment amounts match
val totalPaid = 500 + 129 + 198 + 790
println(s"Total paid: $$$totalPaid (matches reservation total: ${totalPaid == totalFlightPrice})")

// Check user payment methods
val user = getUserDetails("sophia_silva_7557")

println("=== Available Payment Methods ===")
user.paymentMethods.foreach { case (id, method) =>
  method match {
    case cert: PaymentMethod.Certificate => 
      println(s"Certificate $id: $${cert.amount}")
    case gift: PaymentMethod.GiftCard =>
      println(s"Gift Card $id: $${gift.amount}")
    case cc: PaymentMethod.CreditCard =>
      println(s"Credit Card $id: ${cc.brand} ending in ${cc.lastFour}")
  }
}

// Calculate total available funds
val totalCertificateAmount = user.paymentMethods.collect {
  case (_, PaymentMethod.Certificate(_, amount)) => amount
}.sum

val totalGiftCardAmount = user.paymentMethods.collect {
  case (_, PaymentMethod.GiftCard(_, amount)) => amount
}.sum

println(s"\nTotal Certificate funds: $$$totalCertificateAmount")
println(s"Total Gift Card funds: $$$totalGiftCardAmount")
println(s"Total available non-credit funds: $$${totalCertificateAmount + totalGiftCardAmount}")
println(s"Total upgrade cost needed: $1,387")

// Calculate total upgrade charges to credit card
val upgradeReservations = List("NM1VX1", "KC18K6", "H8Q05L")

val upgradeCharges = upgradeReservations.map { resId =>
  val res = getReservationDetails(resId)
  val creditCardPayments = res.paymentHistory.filter(_.paymentId == "credit_card_4196779")
  val totalCreditCardCharge = creditCardPayments.map(_.amount).sum
  (resId, totalCreditCardCharge)
}

println("=== UPGRADE CHARGES TO CREDIT CARD ===")

  println(s"Reservation $resId: $$$charge")

// Check Headphones variants
val headphonesVariants = headphonesProduct.variants
val availableHeadphones = headphonesVariants.filter { case (_, v) => v.available }
val cheapHeadphones = availableHeadphones.filter { case (_, v) => v.price < 100.0 }

println("=== HEADPHONES ===")
println(s"Product: ${headphonesProduct.name}")
println(s"Total variants: ${headphonesVariants.size}")
println(s"Available variants: ${availableHeadphones.size}")
println(s"Available under 100: ${cheapHeadphones.size}")

// Check Wireless Earbuds variants  
val earbudsVariants = earbudsProduct.variants
val availableEarbuds = earbudsVariants.filter { case (_, v) => v.available }
val cheapEarbuds = availableEarbuds.filter { case (_, v) => v.price < 100.0 }

println("\n=== WIRELESS EARBUDS ===")
println(s"Product: ${earbudsProduct.name}")
println(s"Total variants: ${earbudsVariants.size}")
println(s"Available variants: ${availableEarbuds.size}")
println(s"Available under 100: ${cheapEarbuds.size}")

// Check all products for any under $100
println("\n=== CHECKING ALL PRODUCT TYPES FOR ITEMS UNDER $100 ===")
var foundCheapProducts = List.empty[(String, String, Double)] // (product name, item id, price)

// Check a few more products that might be cheaper
val potentialCheapProducts = List(
  "Water Bottle" -> "8310926033",
  "T-Shirt" -> "9523456873", 
  "Notebook" -> "2892623495",
  "Yoga Mat" -> "4635925001",
  "Desk Lamp" -> "6817146515",
  "LED Light Bulb" -> "2696197613"
)

for ((name, id) <- potentialCheapProducts) {
  try {
    val product = getProductDetails(id)
    val cheapVariants = product.variants.values.filter(v => v.available && v.price < 100.0)
    if (cheapVariants.nonEmpty) {
      val cheapest = cheapVariants.minBy(_.price)
      foundCheapProducts = foundCheapProducts :+ (name, cheapest.itemId, cheapest.price)
      println(s"Found: $name has variants under $100 (cheapest: $${cheapest.price})")
    } else {
      println(s"$name: No variants under $100")
    }
  } catch {
    case e: Exception => println(s"Error checking $name: $e")
  }
}

println("\nFound cheap products:")
foundCheapProducts.foreach { case (name, itemId, price) =>
  println(s"  $name - Item ID: $itemId - Price: $${price}")
}

val currentPricePerItem = 94.8
val ceramicPrice = 101.12
val glass15Price = 109.58

val totalCurrentPrice = currentPricePerItem * 2
val totalNewPrice = ceramicPrice + glass15Price
val priceDifference = totalNewPrice - totalCurrentPrice

println(s"New total price: $$$totalNewPrice")

println(s"Your gift card balance: $17.00")

if (priceDifference > 0) {
  println(s"You would need to pay an additional $$$priceDifference")
  if (priceDifference > 17.0) {
    println("WARNING: Your gift card balance of $17.00 is insufficient to cover the price difference.")
  } else {
    println("Your gift card has sufficient balance to cover the price difference.")
  }
} else if (priceDifference < 0) {
  println(s"You would receive a refund of $$${-priceDifference}")
} else {
  println("There is no price difference.")
}

val newItem = variants("2060066974")

println(s"Current item (9354168549): red, XXL, crew neck - Price: $${oldItem.price}")
println(s"New item (2060066974): black, XL, crew neck - Price: $${newItem.price}")

val priceDiff = newItem.price - oldItem.price
if (priceDiff > 0) {
  println(s"\nPrice difference: $${priceDiff} (you would need to pay this amount)")
} else if (priceDiff < 0) {
  println(s"\nPrice difference: $${-priceDiff} (you would receive this refund)")
} else {
  println(s"\nPrice difference: $0 (no payment needed)")
}

println("\n" + "="*50 + "\n")
println("Exchange Summary:")
println("1. Order: #W3388163")
println("2. Exchange: Item 9354168549 (red XXL crew neck) → Item 2060066974 (black XL crew neck)")
println(s"3. Price difference: $${if (priceDiff > 0) priceDiff else -priceDiff} ${if (priceDiff > 0) "to pay" else "refund"}")
println("4. Payment method: PayPal (paypal_5334408)")
println("\nAfter confirmation, you'll receive an email with instructions on how to return the item.")

CASE 241
File: deepseek-v3.2_scala_retail.json | Task: 36 | Trial: 4
================================================================================

LLM OUTPUT (Scala code):
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Find cheapest available variant for each product
println("Finding cheapest available variants for each product...")
println("=" * 50)

var totalSavings = 0.0
var newTotal = total
val currentItems = items
val itemModifications = scala.collection.mutable.ListBuffer[(String, String, Double, Double)]() // (oldItemId, newItemId, oldPrice, newPrice)

for (currentItem <- currentItems) {
  val productId = currentItem.productId
  val productDetails = getProductDetails(productId)
  
  // Find cheapest available variant
  val cheapestVariant = productDetails.variants.values
    .filter(_.available)
    .minBy(_.price)
  
  val oldPrice = currentItem.price
  val newPrice = cheapestVariant.price
  val savings = oldPrice - newPrice
  
  println(s"\n${currentItem.name}:")
  println(s"  Current: Item ${currentItem.itemId} - $$$oldPrice")
  println(s"  Cheapest: Item ${cheapestVariant.itemId} - $$$newPrice (saves: $$$savings)")
  println(s"  Options: ${cheapestVariant.options}")
  
  if (currentItem.itemId != cheapestVariant.itemId) {
    itemModifications += ((currentItem.itemId, cheapestVariant.itemId, oldPrice, newPrice))
    totalSavings += savings
  } else {
    println(s"  (Already the cheapest option)")
  }
}

newTotal = total - totalSavings
println("\n" + "=" * 50)
println(s"Current order total: $$$total")
println(s"Total savings if switching to cheapest options: $$$totalSavings")
println(s"New total would be: $$$newTotal")
println(s"Your card limit: $$$1131")
println(s"Difference: $$${newTotal - 1131}")

if (itemModifications.nonEmpty) {
  println("\nItems that would be modified:")
  itemModifications.foreach { case (oldId, newId, oldPrice, newPrice) =>
    println(s"  Item $oldId ($$$oldPrice) -> Item $newId ($$$newPrice)")
  }
}
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

COMPILER ERROR:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Error: ----------------------------------------------------------------------
41 |println(s"Your card limit: $$$1131")
   |                             ^
   |invalid string interpolation: `$$`, `$"`, `$`ident or `$`BlockExpr expected
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

println("=" * 50)

var totalSavings = 0.0
var newTotal = total
val currentItems = items
val itemModifications = scala.collection.mutable.ListBuffer[(String, String, Double, Double)]() // (oldItemId, newItemId, oldPrice, newPrice)

for (currentItem <- currentItems) {
  val productId = currentItem.productId
  val productDetails = getProductDetails(productId)
  
  // Find cheapest available variant
  val cheapestVariant = productDetails.variants.values
    .filter(_.available)
    .minBy(_.price)
  
  val oldPrice = currentItem.price
  val newPrice = cheapestVariant.price
  val savings = oldPrice - newPrice
  
  println(s"\n${currentItem.name}:")
  println(s"  Current: Item ${currentItem.itemId} - $${oldPrice}")
  println(s"  Cheapest: Item ${cheapestVariant.itemId} - $${newPrice} (saves: $${savings})")
  println(s"  Options: ${cheapestVariant.options}")
  
  if (currentItem.itemId != cheapestVariant.itemId) {
    itemModifications += ((currentItem.itemId, cheapestVariant.itemId, oldPrice, newPrice))
    totalSavings += savings
  } else {
    println(s"  (Already the cheapest option)")
  }
}

newTotal = total - totalSavings
println("\n" + "=" * 50)
println(s"Current order total: $${total}")
println(s"Total savings if switching to cheapest options: $${totalSavings}")
println(s"New total would be: $${newTotal}")

  println("\nItems that would be modified:")
  itemModifications.foreach { case (oldId, newId, oldPrice, newPrice) =>

println("Available bookshelves close to $537.01 (your current bookshelf price):")
println(s"Your current bookshelf: Item ID: 4894369688, Options: glass, brown, 5 ft, Price: $537.01")
println()

val bookshelfPrices = sortedBookshelves.map { case (id, variant) => 
  (id, variant.options, variant.price)
}

// Find bookshelves within $50 of current price
val similarPriceRange = bookshelfPrices.filter { case (_, _, price) => 
  math.abs(price - 537.01) <= 50
}

println("Bookshelves within $50 of your current price ($537.01):")
similarPriceRange.foreach { case (id, options, price) =>
  val diff = price - 537.01
  val sign = if (diff >= 0) "+" else ""
  println(s"Item ID: $id, Options: $options, Price: $$$price (${sign}$$${"%.2f".format(math.abs(diff))})")
}

println()
println("Other available bookshelves (sorted by price):")
bookshelfPrices.foreach { case (id, options, price) =>
  println(s"Item ID: $id, Options: $options, Price: $$$price")
}

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Error: ----------------------------------------------------------------------

CASE 254
File: deepseek-v3.2_scala_retail.json | Task: 38 | Trial: 5

LLM OUTPUT (Scala code):
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Parse the product details to find cheapest available variants
import scala.util.Try

case class ProductSummary(name: String, productId: String, currentItemId: String, currentPrice: Double, cheapestItemId: String, cheapestPrice: Double)

// Helper function to parse product details
def parseProductDetails(productDetails: (String, Any)): ProductSummary = {
  val (pid, details) = productDetails
  
  // Get current item for this product
  val currentItem = items.find(_.productId == pid).get
  
  // Parse the product details string to extract variants
  val detailsStr = details.toString
  
  // Extract variant information using regex
  val variantPattern = """Variant\((\d+),.*?available = (true|false), price = (\d+\.?\d*)\)""".r
  
  val variants = variantPattern.findAllMatchIn(detailsStr).map { m =>
    (m.group(1), m.group(2).toBoolean, m.group(3).toDouble)
  }.toList
  
  // Find cheapest available variant
  val cheapestAvailable = variants.filter(_._2 == true).minByOption(_._3)
  
  ProductSummary(
    name = currentItem.name,
    productId = pid,
    currentItemId = currentItem.itemId,
    currentPrice = currentItem.price,
    cheapestItemId = cheapestAvailable.map(_._1).getOrElse(currentItem.itemId),
    cheapestPrice = cheapestAvailable.map(_._3).getOrElse(currentItem.price)
  )
}

// Parse each product
val productSummaries = productDetails.collect {
  case (pid, prod: Product) => parseProductDetails((pid, prod.toString))
}

println("Current vs Cheapest Available Prices:")
println("=" * 80)
productSummaries.foreach { ps =>
  val savings = ps.currentPrice - ps.cheapestPrice
  println(s"${ps.name}:")
  println(s"  Current: $${ps.currentPrice} (Item ID: ${ps.currentItemId})")
  println(s"  Cheapest available: $${ps.cheapestPrice} (Item ID: ${ps.cheapestItemId})")
  println(s"  Potential savings: $$$savings")
  println()
}

// Calculate total savings and new total
val currentTotal = items.map(_.price).sum
val newTotalWithCheapest = productSummaries.map(_.cheapestPrice).sum
val totalSavings = currentTotal - newTotalWithCheapest

println("=" * 80)
println(s"Current order total: $$$currentTotal")
println(s"Total with cheapest variants: $$$newTotalWithCheapest")
println(s"Total potential savings: $$$totalSavings")
println()

// Check if new total is $950 or below
if (newTotalWithCheapest <= 950) {
  println(s"✓ YES! By switching to cheapest variants, the total would be $$$newTotalWithCheapest (≤ $950)")
} else {
  println(s"✗ NO. Even with cheapest variants, the total would be $$$newTotalWithCheapest (> $950)")
}
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

COMPILER ERROR:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Error: ----------------------------------------------------------------------
65 |  println(s"✓ YES! By switching to cheapest variants, the total would be $$$newTotalWithCheapest (≤ $950)")
   |                                                                                                    ^
   |invalid string interpolation: `$$`, `$"`, `$`ident or `$`BlockExpr expected
-- Error: ----------------------------------------------------------------------

// Parse the product details to find cheapest available variants
import scala.util.Try

case class ProductSummary(name: String, productId: String, currentItemId: String, currentPrice: Double, cheapestItemId: String, cheapestPrice: Double)

// Helper function to parse product details
def parseProductDetails(productDetails: (String, Any)): ProductSummary = {
  val (pid, details) = productDetails
  
  // Get current item for this product
  val currentItem = items.find(_.productId == pid).get
  
  // Parse the product details string to extract variants
  val detailsStr = details.toString
  
  // Extract variant information using regex
  val variantPattern = """Variant\((\d+),.*?available = (true|false), price = (\d+\.?\d*)\)""".r
  
  val variants = variantPattern.findAllMatchIn(detailsStr).map { m =>
    (m.group(1), m.group(2).toBoolean, m.group(3).toDouble)
  }.toList
  
  // Find cheapest available variant
  val cheapestAvailable = variants.filter(_._2 == true).minByOption(_._3)
  
  ProductSummary(
    name = currentItem.name,
    productId = pid,
    currentItemId = currentItem.itemId,
    currentPrice = currentItem.price,
    cheapestItemId = cheapestAvailable.map(_._1).getOrElse(currentItem.itemId),
    cheapestPrice = cheapestAvailable.map(_._3).getOrElse(currentItem.price)
  )
}

// Parse each product
val productSummaries = productDetails.collect {
  case (pid, prod: Product) => parseProductDetails((pid, prod.toString))
}

println("Current vs Cheapest Available Prices:")
println("=" * 80)
productSummaries.foreach { ps =>
  val savings = ps.currentPrice - ps.cheapestPrice
  println(s"${ps.name}:")
  println(f"  Current: $$${ps.currentPrice}%.2f (Item ID: ${ps.currentItemId})")
  println(f"  Cheapest available: $$${ps.cheapestPrice}%.2f (Item ID: ${ps.cheapestItemId})")
  println(f"  Potential savings: $$$savings%.2f")
  println()
}

// Calculate total savings and new total
val currentTotal = items.map(_.price).sum
val newTotalWithCheapest = productSummaries.map(_.cheapestPrice).sum
val totalSavings = currentTotal - newTotalWithCheapest

println("=" * 80)
println(f"Current order total: $$$currentTotal%.2f")
println(f"Total with cheapest variants: $$$newTotalWithCheapest%.2f")
println(f"Total potential savings: $$$totalSavings%.2f")
println()

// Check if new total is $950 or below
if (newTotalWithCheapest <= 950) {
  println(f"✓ YES! By switching to cheapest variants, the total would be $$$newTotalWithCheapest%.2f (≤ $$$950%.2f)")
} else {
  println(f"✗ NO. Even with cheapest variants, the total would be $$$newTotalWithCheapest%.2f (> $$$950%.2f)")
}

// Parse the product details to find cheapest available variants
import scala.util.Try

case class ProductSummary(name: String, productId: String, currentItemId: String, currentPrice: Double, cheapestItemId: String, cheapestPrice: Double)

// Helper function to parse product details
def parseProductDetails(productDetails: (String, Any)): ProductSummary = {
  val (pid, details) = productDetails
  
  // Get current item for this product
  val currentItem = items.find(_.productId == pid).get
  
  // Parse the product details string to extract variants
  val detailsStr = details.toString
  
  // Extract variant information using regex
  val variantPattern = """Variant\((\d+),.*?available = (true|false), price = (\d+\.?\d*)\)""".r
  
  val variants = variantPattern.findAllMatchIn(detailsStr).map { m =>
    (m.group(1), m.group(2).toBoolean, m.group(3).toDouble)
  }.toList
  
  // Find cheapest available variant
  val cheapestAvailable = variants.filter(_._2 == true).minByOption(_._3)
  
  ProductSummary(
    name = currentItem.name,
    productId = pid,
    currentItemId = currentItem.itemId,
    currentPrice = currentItem.price,
    cheapestItemId = cheapestAvailable.map(_._1).getOrElse(currentItem.itemId),
    cheapestPrice = cheapestAvailable.map(_._3).getOrElse(currentItem.price)
  )
}

// Parse each product
val productSummaries = productDetails.collect {
  case (pid, prod: Product) => parseProductDetails((pid, prod.toString))
}

println("Current vs Cheapest Available Prices:")
println("=" * 80)
productSummaries.foreach { ps =>
  val savings = ps.currentPrice - ps.cheapestPrice
  println(s"${ps.name}:")
  println(s"  Current: $${ps.currentPrice} (Item ID: ${ps.currentItemId})")
  println(s"  Cheapest available: $${ps.cheapestPrice} (Item ID: ${ps.cheapestItemId})")
  println(s"  Potential savings: $$$savings")
  println()
}

// Calculate total savings and new total

val newTotalWithCheapest = productSummaries.map(_.cheapestPrice).sum

// 2. Air Purifier - 9534205511 - $473.43 (returning)

val totalNewPrice = newEspressoPrice + newLaptopPrice

  println(s"You would receive a refund of: $$${-priceDifference}")

// Parse the product details to find cheapest available variants
import scala.util.Try

// Helper function to parse product from string
def parseProductDetails(details: Any): Option[Product] = details match {
  case p: Product => Some(p)
  case s: String => None
  case _ => None
}

// Find cheapest available variant for each product
val cheapestVariants = productDetails.flatMap { case (pid, details) =>
  parseProductDetails(details).map { product =>
    val cheapest = product.variants.values
      .filter(_.available)
      .minByOption(_.price)
    (pid, product.name, cheapest)
  }
}

println("Cheapest available variants for each product:")
cheapestVariants.foreach { case (pid, name, cheapestOpt) =>
  cheapestOpt match {
    case Some(variant) =>
      println(s"$name (Product ID: $pid):")
      println(s"  Item ID: ${variant.itemId}")
      println(s"  Price: $${variant.price}")
      println(s"  Options: ${variant.options}")
    case None =>
      println(s"$name (Product ID: $pid): No available variants found")
  }
}

// Calculate total with cheapest variants
val originalItems = items
val currentTotal = originalItems.map(_.price).sum
println(s"\nCurrent order total: $$$currentTotal")

val cheapestTotal = cheapestVariants.flatMap(_._3).map(_.price).sum
println(s"Cheapest possible total: $$$cheapestTotal")

// Check if we can get under $950
if (cheapestTotal <= 950.0) {
  println(s"✓ Cheapest total ($$$cheapestTotal) is under $$$950")
} else {
  println(s"✗ Cheapest total ($$$cheapestTotal) is still over $$$950")
}
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

COMPILER ERROR:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Error: ----------------------------------------------------------------------

   |                                                           ^
   |invalid string interpolation: `$$`, `$"`, `$`ident or `$`BlockExpr expected

   |                                                                ^
   |invalid string interpolation: `$$`, `$"`, `$`ident or `$`BlockExpr expected

println("\nCheapest available alternatives with prices:")

println(s"Action Camera: Current $$${currentActionCameraPrice} -> Alternative $$${cheapestActionCamera.price} (Item ID: ${cheapestActionCamera.itemId}, Options: ${cheapestActionCamera.options})")

// Desk Lamp  
val cheapestDeskLamp = cheaperDeskLamps.minBy(_.price)
println(s"Desk Lamp: Current $$${currentDeskLampPrice} -> Alternative $$${cheapestDeskLamp.price} (Item ID: ${cheapestDeskLamp.itemId}, Options: ${cheapestDeskLamp.options})")
