val cheapestTshirt = cheaperTshirts.minBy(_.price)
println(s"T-Shirt: Current $$${currentTshirtPrice} -> Alternative $$${cheapestTshirt.price} (Item ID: ${cheapestTshirt.itemId}, Options: ${cheapestTshirt.options})")

println("\nNo cheaper alternatives available for Patio Umbrella or Backpack")

// Calculate potential savings if we switch all possible items
val actionCameraSavings = currentActionCameraPrice - cheapestActionCamera.price
val deskLampSavings = currentDeskLampPrice - cheapestDeskLamp.price
val tshirtSavings = currentTshirtPrice - cheapestTshirt.price
val totalPossibleSavings = actionCameraSavings + deskLampSavings + tshirtSavings
val newPotentialTotal = currentTotal - totalPossibleSavings

println(s"\nPotential savings:")
println(s"  Action Camera: $${actionCameraSavings}")
println(s"  Desk Lamp: $${deskLampSavings}")
println(s"  T-Shirt: $${tshirtSavings}")
println(s"  Total possible savings: $${totalPossibleSavings}")
println(s"  New potential total: $${newPotentialTotal}")

// Check if this gets us under $1131
if (newPotentialTotal <= 1131) {
  println("\n✓ Switching to these cheaper alternatives would bring your total under $1131!")
} else {
  println(s"\n✗ Even with these changes, your total would be $$${newPotentialTotal}, which is still above $1131.")
}

================================================================================

LLM OUTPUT (Scala code):
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Now let's analyze the cheapest available options for each product
case class CheapestOption(productId: String, productName: String, currentItemId: String, cheapestItemId: String, currentPrice: Double, cheapestPrice: Double, options: Map[String, String])

val currentOrder = getOrderDetails("#W9348897")

// For each item in the order, find the cheapest available variant
val cheapestOptions = currentOrder.items.map { item =>
  val productDetails = getProductDetails(item.productId)
  val variants = productDetails.variants.values.toList
  
  // Filter to only available variants
  val availableVariants = variants.filter(_.available)
  
  // Find the cheapest available variant
  val cheapestVariant = availableVariants.minBy(_.price)
  
  CheapestOption(
    productId = item.productId,
    productName = item.name,
    currentItemId = item.itemId,
    cheapestItemId = cheapestVariant.itemId,
    currentPrice = item.price,
    cheapestPrice = cheapestVariant.price,
    options = cheapestVariant.options
  )
}

println("Current order items and their cheapest available alternatives:")
println("-" * 80)
cheapestOptions.foreach { opt =>
  println(s"\n${opt.productName}:")
  println(s"  Current: Item ${opt.currentItemId}, Price: $$${opt.currentPrice}")
  println(s"  Cheapest: Item ${opt.cheapestItemId}, Price: $$${opt.cheapestPrice}")
  println(s"  Options: ${opt.options.map { case (k, v) => s"$k=$v" }.mkString(", ")}")
  println(s"  Savings: $${opt.currentPrice - opt.cheapestPrice}")
}

val currentTotal = currentOrder.items.map(_.price).sum
val potentialTotal = cheapestOptions.map(_.cheapestPrice).sum
val potentialSavings = currentTotal - potentialTotal

println("\n" + "-" * 80)
println(s"Current total: $$$currentTotal")
println(s"Potential total with cheapest options: $$$potentialTotal")
println(s"Potential savings: $$$potentialSavings")
println(s"Would be under $$$1150: ${potentialTotal < 1150}")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

   |                           ^
   |invalid string interpolation: `$$`, `$"`, `$`ident or `$`BlockExpr expected

  if (variant.available && variant.price < 300.0) {
    count += 1
    println(s"${count}. Item ID: $itemId")
    println(s"   Price: $${variant.price}")
    println(s"   Options: ${variant.options}")
    println()
  }
}

  println("No available Bluetooth speakers under $300 found.")
} else {
  println(s"Total found: $count available options under $300")

// Parse the product details to find cheapest available variants
import scala.util.Using
import java.io.StringReader
import play.api.libs.json._

// Helper function to parse product details
def parseProductDetails(productDetails: String): (String, List[(String, Double, Map[String, String])]) = {
  // Extract product name and variants
  val lines = productDetails.split("\n")
  val productName = lines.head.split("\\(")(1).split(",")(0)
  
  // Parse variants - looking for lines with "Variant("
  val variants = lines.filter(_.contains("Variant(")).map { line =>
    val variantPattern = """Variant\((\d+),Map\(([^)]+)\),([^,]+),([^)]+)\)""".r
    line match {
      case variantPattern(itemId, optionsStr, availability, price) =>
        val isAvailable = availability.trim == "true"
        val priceValue = price.trim.toDouble
        val options = optionsStr.split(",").map { opt =>
          val parts = opt.split(" -> ")
          if (parts.length == 2) parts(0).trim -> parts(1).trim
          else "" -> ""
        }.filter(_._1.nonEmpty).toMap
        
        (itemId, priceValue, options, isAvailable)
    }
  }.filter(_._4).map(v => (v._1, v._2, v._3)).toList
  
  (productName, variants)
}

// Get cheapest variants for each product
val productDetailsList = List(
  getProductDetails("3377618313"),
  getProductDetails("9743693396"),
  getProductDetails("6817146515"),
  getProductDetails("9523456873"),
  getProductDetails("2524789262")
)

var totalCheapestPrice = 0.0
val cheapestVariants = productDetailsList.map { details =>
  val (productName, variants) = parseProductDetails(details)
  if (variants.isEmpty) {
    (productName, None, 0.0)
  } else {
    val cheapest = variants.minBy(_._2)
    totalCheapestPrice += cheapest._2
    (productName, Some(cheapest._1), cheapest._2)
  }
}

println("Cheapest available variants for each product:")
println("=" * 50)
cheapestVariants.foreach { case (productName, itemIdOpt, price) =>
  itemIdOpt match {
    case Some(itemId) => println(f"$productName: Item ID $itemId - $$$price%.2f")
    case None => println(s"$productName: No available variants")
  }
}
println("=" * 50)
println(f"Total with cheapest variants: $$$totalCheapestPrice%.2f")
println(f"Current order total: $1166.98")
println(f"Difference: $$${1166.98 - totalCheapestPrice}%.2f")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

COMPILER ERROR:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Error: ----------------------------------------------------------------------
63 |println(f"Current order total: $1166.98")
   |                               ^
   |invalid string interpolation: `$$`, `$"`, `$`ident or `$`BlockExpr expected
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

// Parse the product details to find cheapest available variants
case class CheapestVariant(productId: String, currentItemId: String, cheapestItemId: String, currentPrice: Double, cheapestPrice: Double)

val orderItems = List(
  ("Action Camera", "3377618313", "6117189161", 481.5),
  ("Patio Umbrella", "9743693396", "9879255677", 288.82),
  ("Desk Lamp", "6817146515", "7453605304", 150.01),
  ("T-Shirt", "9523456873", "3799046073", 53.27),
  ("Backpack", "2524789262", "9851293632", 193.38)
)

val cheapestVariants = orderItems.map { case (name, productId, currentItemId, currentPrice) =>
  val product = productDetails.find(_._1 == productId).get._2
  val availableVariants = product.variants.filter { case (_, variant) => variant.available }
  val cheapestVariant = availableVariants.values.minBy(_.price)
  
  CheapestVariant(productId, currentItemId, cheapestVariant.itemId, currentPrice, cheapestVariant.price)
}

println("Current items and cheapest available alternatives:")
println("-" * 80)
cheapestVariants.foreach { cv =>
  println(s"Product: ${orderItems.find(_._2 == cv.productId).get._1}")
  println(s"  Current item: ${cv.currentItemId} - Price: $$${cv.currentPrice}")
  println(s"  Cheapest available: ${cv.cheapestItemId} - Price: $$${cv.cheapestPrice}")
  println(s"  Savings: $${cv.currentPrice - cv.cheapestPrice}")
  println()
}

val currentTotal = orderItems.map(_._4).sum
val newTotal = cheapestVariants.map(_.cheapestPrice).sum
val totalSavings = currentTotal - newTotal

println(s"Current total: $$$currentTotal")
println(s"New total with cheapest variants: $$$newTotal")
println(s"Total savings: $$$totalSavings")
println(s"Your credit limit: $$$1131")
println(s"Difference: $${1131 - newTotal}")

// Wait, I need to use the ORIGINAL business prices from the reservation vs current economy prices
// Let me recalculate using the original prices paid

// From reservation details - original prices paid:
// JG7FMM: HAT028 ($1859) + HAT277 ($1679) = $3538 for 2 passengers = $1769 per person
// 2FBBAH: HAT080 ($537) + HAT076 ($996) + HAT255 ($1440) + HAT148 ($1417) = $3390 for 1 person
// X7BYG1: HAT232 ($1505) + HAT228 ($1519) = $3024 for 2 passengers = $1512 per person
// EQ1G6C: HAT084 ($1820) + HAT175 ($940) = $2760 for 1 person
// BOH180: HAT276 ($1981) + HAT279 ($820) = $2801 for 2 passengers = $1400.50 per person

// Current economy prices (from search):

  }
}

    val total = 109.58 + price
    val diff = total - originalPrice
    println(s"  9647374798 (Glass, 1.5L, Gas) $109.58 + $id ($mat, $cap, $stove) $price = $total (Difference: ${if(diff > 0) "pay $" + "%.2f".format(diff) else "refund $" + "%.2f".format(-diff)})")

// Calculate the cheapest business class options
// Outbound: HAT023 (JFK to SFO) - Business: $364 per person

// For return, we have several options:
// Option 1: HAT204 (SFO to SEA) + HAT021 (SEA to JFK) = $248 + $453 = $701 per person
// Option 2: HAT204 (SFO to SEA) + HAT100 (SEA to JFK) = $248 + $259 = $507 per person
// Option 3: HAT082 (SFO to IAH) + HAT085 (IAH to JFK) = $404 + $352 = $756 per person

// The cheapest return is Option 2: HAT204 + HAT100 = $507 per person

val outboundPrice = 364
val returnPrice = 507
val pricePerPerson = outboundPrice + returnPrice
val totalFor3Passengers = pricePerPerson * 3

println(s"Cheapest Business Class Round Trip Option:")
println(s"Outbound: HAT023 (JFK to SFO on May 26) - $${outboundPrice} per person")

// Current reservation costs
val currentOutbound1 = 177  // HAT085
val currentOutbound2 = 146  // HAT023
val currentReturn = 180     // HAT278 (old date)
val currentTotal = currentOutbound1 + currentOutbound2 + currentReturn

println("Current Reservation Costs:")
println(s"HAT085 (May 18): $177")
println(s"HAT023 (May 18): $146")
println(s"HAT278 (May 22): $180")
println(s"Current Total: $currentTotal")
println("\n" + "="*50 + "\n")

// New flight costs
val newOutbound = 282      // HAT072 (May 19, Business)
val newReturn = 443        // HAT278 (May 23, Business)
val newFlightTotal = newOutbound + newReturn

println("New Flight Costs (Business Class):")
println(s"HAT072 (May 19, Business): $282")
println(s"HAT278 (May 23, Business): $443")
println(s"New Flight Total: $newFlightTotal")
println("\n" + "="*50 + "\n")

// Baggage costs
val freeBagsForBusiness = 3  // Gold member gets 3 free bags per business passenger
val totalBagsRequested = 2
val nonFreeBags = if (totalBagsRequested > freeBagsForBusiness) totalBagsRequested - freeBagsForBusiness else 0
val baggageCost = nonFreeBags * 50

println("Baggage Analysis:")
println(s"You're booking Business class")
println(s"Free checked bags for business: $freeBagsForBusiness")
println(s"Bags you want to add: $totalBagsRequested")
println(s"Non-free bags: $nonFreeBags")
println(s"Baggage cost: $baggageCost")
println("\n" + "="*50 + "\n")

// Calculate difference
val flightDifference = newFlightTotal - currentTotal
val totalCostDifference = flightDifference + baggageCost

println("Cost Summary:")
println(s"Current reservation total: $currentTotal")
println(s"New flights total: $newFlightTotal")
println(s"Flight cost difference: $flightDifference")
println(s"Baggage cost: $baggageCost")
println(s"Total additional cost: $totalCostDifference")
println("\n" + "="*50 + "\n")

// Check against gift card balance
val giftCardBalance = 533
val amountNeeded = totalCostDifference
println(s"Your gift card balance: $giftCardBalance")
println(s"Amount needed for changes: $amountNeeded")
if (amountNeeded > 0) {
  println(s"You will need to pay: $amountNeeded")
} else {
  println(s"You will receive a refund of: ${-amountNeeded}")
}

// Calculate the cheapest business class combination
// For 3 passengers

// LEG 1: JFK to SFO on May 26
// Direct: HAT023 = $364 per person
// One-stop options:
// HAT069 + HAT011 = $470 + $368 = $838 per person
// HAT069 + HAT258 = $470 + $363 = $833 per person
// HAT069 + HAT274 = $470 + $310 = $780 per person
// HAT083 + HAT011 = $461 + $368 = $829 per person
// HAT083 + HAT258 = $461 + $363 = $824 per person
// HAT083 + HAT274 = $461 + $310 = $771 per person
// HAT083 + HAT107 = $461 + $446 = $907 per person

val leg1Cheapest = 364 // HAT023 direct

// LEG 2: SFO to SEA on May 28
// Direct: HAT204 = $248 per person
// One-stop options:
// HAT134 + HAT045 = $210 + $370 = $580 per person
// HAT134 + HAT251 = $210 + $218 = $428 per person (but HAT251 has 0 business seats)
// HAT134 + HAT156 = $210 + $257 = $467 per person

val leg2Cheapest = 248 // HAT204 direct

// LEG 3: SEA to JFK on May 28
// Direct options:
// HAT021 = $453 per person
// HAT089 = $477 per person
// HAT100 = $259 per person
// HAT276 = $430 per person
// One-stop:
// HAT220 + HAT233 = $304 + $377 = $681 per person

val leg3Cheapest = 259 // HAT100 direct

val totalPerPerson = leg1Cheapest + leg2Cheapest + leg3Cheapest
val totalFor3Passengers = totalPerPerson * 3

println(s"Cheapest Business Class Combination:")
println(s"Leg 1 (JFK→SFO): HAT023 - $${leg1Cheapest} per person")
println(s"Leg 2 (SFO→SEA): HAT204 - $${leg2Cheapest} per person")
println(s"Leg 3 (SEA→JFK): HAT100 - $${leg3Cheapest} per person")
println(s"\nTotal per person: $${totalPerPerson}")
println(s"Total for 3 passengers: $${totalFor3Passengers}")
println(s"\nYour current reservation cost: $189")
println(s"Price difference: $${totalFor3Passengers - 189}")

// Current reservation costs
val currentFlight1Price = 122
val currentFlight2Price = 127
val currentTotalPerPassenger = currentFlight1Price + currentFlight2Price
val currentTotalFor2Passengers = currentTotalPerPassenger * 2

println(s"Current booking (Economy):")
println(s"  Flight HAT235: $122 per passenger")
println(s"  Flight HAT298: $127 per passenger")
println(s"  Total per passenger: $currentTotalPerPassenger")
println(s"  Total for 2 passengers: $currentTotalFor2Passengers")
println()

// New business class prices
val newFlight1Price = 350  // HAT235 business
val newFlight2Price = 499  // HAT298 business
val newTotalPerPassenger = newFlight1Price + newFlight2Price
val newTotalFor2Passengers = newTotalPerPassenger * 2

println(s"New booking (Business):")
println(s"  Flight HAT235: $350 per passenger")
println(s"  Flight HAT298: $499 per passenger")
println(s"  Total per passenger: $newTotalPerPassenger")
println(s"  Total for 2 passengers: $newTotalFor2Passengers")
println()

// Calculate upgrade cost
val upgradeCost = newTotalFor2Passengers - currentTotalFor2Passengers
println(s"Upgrade cost: $upgradeCost")
println()

// Baggage calculation for Gold member in Business class
// Gold member gets 4 free checked bags per business passenger
val freebagsPerPassenger = 4
val totalFreebagsFor2Passengers = freebagsPerPassenger * 2
val bagsToAdd = 2
val nonfreeBags = if (bagsToAdd > totalFreebagsFor2Passengers) bagsToAdd - totalFreebagsFor2Passengers else 0
val baggageCost = nonfreeBags * 50

println(s"Baggage calculation:")
println(s"  Gold member in Business: 4 free bags per passenger")
println(s"  Total free bags for 2 passengers: $totalFreebagsFor2Passengers")
println(s"  Bags to add: $bagsToAdd")
println(s"  Non-free bags: $nonfreeBags")
println(s"  Baggage cost: $baggageCost")
println()

val totalCost = upgradeCost + baggageCost
println(s"Total additional cost: $totalCost")

  if (variant.available && variant.price < 94.80) {
    foundCheaper = true
    println(s"\nItem ID: $itemId")
    println(s"  Material: ${variant.options("material")}")
    println(s"  Capacity: ${variant.options("capacity")}")
    println(s"  Stovetop Compatibility: ${variant.options("stovetop compatibility")}")
    println(s"  Price: $${variant.price}")
    println(s"  REFUND: $${94.80 - variant.price} per item")
  }
}

if (!foundCheaper) {
  println("\nNo cheaper options found!")
}

println("\n" + "=" * 60)
println("\nOptions that cost THE SAME (would get no refund, but no extra payment either):")
println("=" * 60)

product.variants.foreach { case (itemId, variant) =>
  if (variant.available && variant.price == 94.80) {
    println(s"\nItem ID: $itemId")
    println(s"  Material: ${variant.options("material")}")
    println(s"  Capacity: ${variant.options("capacity")}")
    println(s"  Stovetop Compatibility: ${variant.options("stovetop compatibility")}")
    println(s"  Price: $${variant.price}")

  ("Action Camera", "6117189161", 481.50),

  ("T-Shirt", "3234800602", 46.66),

// - Action Camera: $481.50 (6117189161) -> cheapest available: $466.75 (6700049080)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Find the cheapest available Desk Lamp variant
val product = getProductDetails("6817146515")
val variants = product.variants

var cheapestAvailable: (String, Double, Map[String, String]) = null

variants.foreach { case (itemId, variant) =>
  if (variant.available) {
    if (cheapestAvailable == null || variant.price < cheapestAvailable._2) {
      cheapestAvailable = (itemId, variant.price, variant.options)
    }
  }
}

println(s"Cheapest available Desk Lamp: Item ID ${cheapestAvailable._1}")
println(s"Price: $${cheapestAvailable._2}")
println(s"Options: ${cheapestAvailable._3}")
println(s"Current item price: $153.23")
println(s"Price difference (refund): ${153.23 - cheapestAvailable._2}")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

COMPILER ERROR:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

18 |println(s"Current item price: $153.23")
   |                              ^
   |invalid string interpolation: `$$`, `$"`, `$`ident or `$`BlockExpr expected
